Page 4

The Dispute Between Yugoslavia and Hungary

League of Nations Mediation Achieves Success

The Executive Yuan Unanimously Approves the Compromise Proposal

Both Parties in the Dispute Express Congratulations

An Eleven-Nation Committee is Formed to Draft a Convention on Punishing Atrocities

(Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council today unanimously passed a compromise proposal to resolve the dispute between Yugoslavia and Hungary. After private talks between Yugoslav Foreign Minister Yevtic, British Lord Privy Seal Eden, Italian representative Aloisi, and French Foreign Minister Laval, it was agreed to accept this proposal. It is expected that this agreement will calm the tension between Yugoslavia and Hungary. (10th Day National Telegram)

(Geneva) The Central European crisis triggered by Yugoslavia's complaint against Hungary regarding the Marseille assassination is gradually subsiding. Hungary accepted the resolution on this matter at today's League of Nations Administrative Council meeting, which stipulates: (1) A general condemnation of terrorism; (2) Hungary should thoroughly investigate the negligence of certain officials and punish them; (3) The League of Nations Administrative Council should establish a committee to consider all issues related to terrorist acts, especially the right to asylum and abuse of political fugitives. (Reuters Telegram)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council tonight unanimously passed a resolution ending the debate on Yugoslavia's application. The resolution first expressed respect for the late Yugoslav King Alexander and the late French Foreign Minister Barthou, who were assassinated in Marseille, and then stated that no country should encourage or tolerate the activities of terrorist factions within its borders for political purposes. Prevention should be taken before terrorist acts occur, and punishment should be imposed afterward without any neglect. Assistance should be provided to other countries upon request, as this is the duty of any country. The Administrative Council, based on the documents submitted by Yugoslavia, felt that various issues related to the existence and activities of terrorist elements outside Yugoslavia had not been properly resolved to the satisfaction of the Yugoslav government, and that some Hungarian officials, at least due to negligence, were responsible for the preparation of the Marseille assassination. The Council believes that the Hungarian government is aware of its international responsibilities, which are to take or promote various measures to sanction officials whose crimes have been confirmed, and believes that the Hungarian government is willing to fulfill this responsibility. It specifically requests that the measures to be taken in the future be notified to the Council at any time. Finally, the Administrative Council resolved to establish a committee of experts to study the issue of drafting an international convention to punish political terrorism and crimes. This committee will be composed of representatives from eleven countries: Belgium, Britain, Chile, Spain, France, Hungary, Italy, Poland, Romania, Switzerland, and the Soviet Union, and will submit a report to the Administrative Council. (10th Day Havas Telegram)

(Geneva) The League of Nations has restored its slightly damaged reputation due to the good results achieved in handling the dispute between Hungary and Yugoslavia and the Saar police affairs. The Administrative Council has extended the meeting to January 10th and will continue to meet during the Saar plebiscite. The Yugoslav Foreign Ministry today expressed satisfaction with the League of Nations' resolution on the Hungarian-Yugoslav dispute. Newspapers in the Yugoslav capital celebrated the resolution, while newspapers in the Hungarian capital also expressed gratitude and praised the resourcefulness of British Lord Privy Seal Eden. (11th Day Reuters Telegram)

Romanian Foreign Minister's Words Shocked the Audience

Chairman Said the League of Nations is Capable

(Geneva) When the League of Nations Administrative Council reopened its meeting this afternoon, Romanian Foreign Minister Titulescu spoke out sharply against Hungary, saying that they had never felt such a loss before the death of Count Albert Apponyi, the former Hungarian representative to the League of Nations. The Count always based his arguments on the beginning of the discussion, while Hungarian critics today are unnecessarily accused of provocation. He resided in Britain and Switzerland for a long time. May I ask whether the history of the two countries allows fugitives to carry weapons and practice with weapons, bullets, and explosives? The Romanian Foreign Minister also told the Hungarians that the honor of the country should be considered in this matter. The council members appeared uneasy when they heard the words of the Romanian Foreign Minister. Italian representative Aloisi stared at the ceiling, French Foreign Minister Laval picked his teeth, and British Lord Privy Seal Eden frequently looked at his fingernails. The Romanian Foreign Minister continued that even if the Hungarian government did not have contact with the Croatian fugitives, it was difficult to absolve itself of negligence in terms of its responsibility. As for the revision of the treaty, it should be known that today, the general public believes that maintaining the status quo is sufficient to appease. Those who are dissatisfied with the current borders account for only a very small number in various countries. The Romanian Foreign Minister finally said that Hungary is the most active and enthusiastic center of the movement to revise the treaty.

According to Croatian Foreign Minister Dr. Pinitis, who took the floor after him, his tone was milder than that of Titulescu. He only opposed the movement to revise the peace treaty and pleaded with the League of Nations Administrative Council to find a way to satisfy Yugoslavia.

Yugoslav Foreign Minister Yevtich declared that Hungary's memorandum in response to Yugoslavia's complaint was entirely denied, and that there was no evidence to support the claim that it was a political tactic of the Little Entente. The South Slavic fugitives established an agency in Hungary for two years, and the Hungarian government only admitted to knowing about it and needed seven months to clean up the agency. Its lack of credibility can be seen from this. The South Slavic government has been complaining to the Hungarian government about terrorist parties for more than five years, but the Hungarian government has only dealt with one case, but the terrorists involved in the case are still at large and escaped before being arrested.

Hungarian representative to the Minority Committee, Eckhardt, stated that the issue of fugitives is gradually deteriorating. The Yugoslav government promised to stop expelling Hungarian expatriates, but has not yet complied.

After the Administrative Council meeting, the representatives held a closed meeting to discuss the wording of the draft resolution. The draft resolution has been telegraphed to its home government by the Hungarian representative and will be formally submitted at tonight's League of Nations Administrative Council meeting.

The compromise reached included blaming the Marseille assassination and stating that no country can ignore any plan to prevent such crimes from being repeated. The debate heard by the League of Nations Administrative Council, and the documents received, all showed that some Hungarian officials were negligent in their duties regarding matters related to the conspiracy that led to the Marseille assassination. The League of Nations Administrative Council hopes that the Hungarian government will fulfill its international obligations and report to the League of Nations Administrative Council with appropriate punishments imposed on weak officials. The League of Nations Administrative Council believes that international law is insufficient to guarantee effective international cooperation regarding the rules for suppressing the activities of terrorist parties, so it decided to establish a committee of experts to study the issue in order to draft an international convention on this matter.

The chairman of the League of Nations Administrative Council declared at the end of today's debate that the League of Nations has proved its ability to handle affairs.

The general public was initially afraid that the Hungarian government would disagree with the issue of the responsibility of some Hungarian officials mentioned in the draft resolution, but it was heard that the Hungarian government had accepted the draft resolution and was very satisfied. (10th Day Reuters Telegram)

Establishment of the Compromise

(Geneva) The League of Nations had a long consultation today regarding the dispute between Yugoslavia and Hungary, among which French Foreign Minister Laval, British representative Eden, and Italian representative Aloisi made the most efforts. It started in the early morning and ended in the afternoon, and a new mediation plan was established. On the one hand, it appeases Yugoslavia's anger, and on the other hand, it does not hurt Hungary's feelings too much. This plan stipulates that (1) a formal and empty crime statement should be announced for the Marseille tragedy, and an international court should be organized to specialize in hearing terrorist acts; (2) the territorial integrity of the League of Nations member states must not be illegally and wantonly invaded, and this point should be recorded in the League of Nations minutes; (3) according to the evidence obtained, Hungary does have negligence in suppressing Croatian terrorist organizations, and the Hungarian government should promptly investigate the responsible officials. At first, various countries thought that the wording of the above draft resolution was flexible and hoped that both South Korea and Hungary would agree. Unexpectedly, when seeking the consent of South Korea and Hungary, both sides insisted on their own opinions and refused to show weakness. Hungary was unwilling to be openly criticized for neglecting suppression, while South Rasfus insisted that the strict punishment of the parties concerned was indispensable. After the mediation of the three major political figures of Britain, France and Italy, the compromise was reached. When the League of Nations Administrative Council reconvened this afternoon, Romanian Director Titulescu again raised severe questions to Hungary. Romania's support for Yugoslavia was expected, but the severity of Titulescu's wording was unexpected. Titulescu continued to mention the issue of amending the treaty, saying that according to Article 19 of the League of Nations Covenant, any amendment to the current treaty must be unanimously passed by all members of the League of Nations, including the countries concerned, so that the amendment of the treaty is legal, and all advocacy of amending the treaty is illegal, because it actually violates the League of Nations Covenant, and the League of Nations Covenant is aimed at protecting the territorial integrity of all countries. (10th Day National Telegram)

(Geneva) France today submitted a memorandum on the conclusion of an international convention stipulating the right of asylum and suppressing abuse to the League of Nations Administrative Council. The memorandum involves terrorism of a political nature, such as attempts to assassinate heads of state, government leaders, public officials, and private individuals with different political views, and opposes sabotage and terrorist groups and propaganda. The memorandum stipulates that any case that violates the international convention may request the International Court of Justice in The Hague to try it, and that any condemned person may only be pardoned by the League of Nations Administrative Council. League of Nations member states should provide extradition facilities for political assassins. The League of Nations Administrative Council seems to be going to appoint a small committee to consider the international convention proposed by France. (10th Day Reuters Telegram)

Great Victory for the League of Nations

(Geneva) The Hungarian government has finalized and accepted the draft resolution of the League of Nations Administrative Council on the Marseille case, and the dispute between South Korea and Hungary has ended from now on. This is a great victory for the League of Nations. At 6:05 this evening, when Czech Foreign Minister Benes gave a speech in the Administrative Council and the interpreter translated it, British Secretary of State Eden, French Foreign Minister Laval, Italian representative Aloisi, and Hungarian Foreign Minister Ganya gathered in another room. The representatives of Britain, France, and Italy made their final efforts to make Hungary agree to the draft resolution that had already been drafted. The hope of a compromise has become even stronger since then. At 11:15 in the evening, the Administrative Council reconvened. Chairman Vasconcelos of Portugal, expressed his respect for the late Yugoslav King Alexander and the late French Foreign Minister Barthou. However, because the Hungarian government's reply had not yet arrived, the meeting was adjourned for a quarter of an hour. After the reply arrived, expressing its support for the draft resolution, the Administrative Council reconvened and unanimously passed the resolution. French Foreign Minister Laval declared after the vote, [The League of Nations is helpful to peace. This can be proved again. The content of the resolution coincides with our psychology, and the League of Nations deeply mourns the national mourning of Yugoslavia, which is also expressed in the resolution. This case explains various principles, proves various facts, and makes judgments. Whether the situation can be eased in the future and meet the wishes of the general public depends only on the Hungarian government. As for the League of Nations Administrative Council, its high mission has been accomplished, which is what we should declare. (10th Day Havas Telegram)

(Geneva) When the League of Nations Administrative Council adjourned last night, French Foreign Minister Laval praised the wise attitude of Hungary and South Korea in approving the resolution, and said that the League of Nations once again lived up to its noble mission and made great contributions to maintaining peace. Following Laval's speech, Italian representative Aloisi and Administrative Council Chairman Vasconcelos of Portugal thanked British representative Eden and then announced the adjournment. The Administrative Council will discuss the Saar issue at today's meeting, and after that, this extraordinary meeting will end. (10th Day Havas Telegram)

The League of Nations Passes a Resolution on the Saar Police Issue

British to be Commander-in-Chief

(Geneva) The League of Nations Administrative Council today unanimously passed a resolution authorizing Knox, chairman of the Saar Governing Commission, to convene an international police force to maintain order during the vote next month. The police force is allocated as follows: (1) 1,500 British; (2) 1,300 Italians; (3) 250 each from the Netherlands and Sweden. All are under the command of British officers, and the candidates have not yet been announced. The Administrative Council will reconvene on January 12, the day before the Saar vote, to discuss the Saar issue. (11th Day National Telegram)

(London) According to Foreign Minister Simon's statement in the House of Commons today, the international police force sent to the Saar to maintain order during the plebiscite will be commanded by British officers, and the team should be able to serve in the Saar before Christmas.

According to a Reuters reporter in Geneva, the Netherlands and Sweden have accepted the League of Nations' request and agreed to send teams to join the international police force. Knox, chairman of the Saar Administrative Commission, is British, so the number of people sent by the United Kingdom will be particularly large. The total number of the police force is 4,000.

According to a Reuters reporter in Rotterdam, the Netherlands, the Dutch government will send 200 marines to the Saar on December 12. (10th Day Reuters Telegram)

Saarbrücken: The international troops sent by the League of Nations to maintain order will arrive here on the 22nd of this month. The Saar Administration Commission has recently started the resettlement work. According to the number of troops, there are about 3,500 people in total. The Saar mining agency's houses can accommodate 2,600 people, and the remaining 900 people should be provided with dormitories by residents, otherwise they must be requisitioned from the private sector. The authorities have considered it. In addition, the International Army enjoys extraterritoriality, and what kind of court should accept disputes between soldiers and residents? The Administrative Committee is now preparing regulations to regulate it. (11th Day Havas Telegram)

There are about 55,000 people who live outside the Saar and are eligible to vote, of which about 48,000 are from Germany, 5,000 are from France, 900 are from the United States and Canada, 200 are from South America, about 30 are from Africa and Asia, and the rest are from European countries. The authorities will distribute certificates printed with banknotes to each voter to prevent counterfeiting. Those who come from Germany have special trains and specially prepared residences. Those who come from other countries will also be free of charge for transportation by car or boat. (11th Day National Telegram)

Current Affairs Commentary

Group Marriages in the New Life

The Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau, in view of the increasingly extravagant social customs and the expenditure on weddings often amounting to thousands, has specially drafted measures for group weddings to promote thrift and reverse the declining trend. The various points proposed are well-intentioned and commendable, truly a good deed to change customs and habits.

Marriage is a major event in life, and also a necessary procedure to maintain the family system and stabilize social life. However, if it is too difficult, it will easily lead to an increase in the number of unmarried men and women. If it is too easy, it will lead to frequent separations of couples and shake the foundation of the family. Both excess and deficiency can become factors that contribute to social evils and endanger the prosperity of the nation. Today, extravagance is prevalent, especially in large cities where ostentation is valued. The cost of weddings often exceeds thousands. The lower and middle classes often incur debts for marriage in order to maintain appearances. Speaking of individuals, they suffer for life; speaking of families, they become dull and lifeless. As a result, some are still unmarried even in their prime, and some live together without marriage because marriage is not easy. As a result, the problem of late marriage in society is becoming increasingly apparent, and illicit relationships between men and women are almost regarded as insignificant. If we browse through newspapers, we see records of adultery cases every day. Although such scandalous events cannot be said to be entirely affected by the difficulty of marriage, there is indeed some connection between the two, which cannot be denied. Its harm to national morality is not insignificant. A nation is a collection of individuals. If individuals cannot lead a healthy life, the entire nation will inevitably decline.

Under the current circumstances, the best way to remedy this is to vigorously promote the ethics of marriage on the one hand, maintaining the solemnity of marriage, and on the other hand, increasing the punishment for adultery. If so, those who are unable to marry easily can enjoy the happiness of family life, and illicit relationships can be reduced accordingly. Now, the group marriage measures proposed by the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau simultaneously address both the promotion of marriage ethics and the maintenance of the solemnity of marriage, which can be said to be a win-win situation. However, the way to promote it still depends on the upper and middle classes of society taking the lead and setting an example, creating a trend. Otherwise, it will still be difficult to sustain it permanently.

Furthermore, according to the measures formulated by the Social Bureau, the wedding dates are only four days a year, and the number of participants in this wedding is limited. After the quota is full, they will be rejected. This kind of restriction is naturally reasonable in places with sparse population, but in this city with dense population, there is still room for discussion. Since ethical marriage is a virtue, universality is of the utmost importance. We believe that, in addition to the review of marriage qualifications, there should be no restrictions. As long as the number is appropriate, the wedding can be held. If the mayor and the director of the Social Bureau are too busy with official duties to officiate the wedding at any time, other bureau directors and respected members of society may share the burden, so that lovers can get married sooner and not sigh at the many obstacles to good things.

Ambassador Guo Hosts Banquet for Inspection Group

Sino-British Goodwill Speeches Published

British Government and Public Pay Attention to China's Situation

Our Two Inspection Groups Receive Preferential Treatment in Britain

(London) Ambassador Guo Taiqi hosted a banquet in his residence today for Yu Pengfei, Xu Tingyao, and Mao Bangchu, and invited British Air Minister Londonderry, Army Minister Hailsham, Transport Minister Piri, Chairman of the China Association Benard, and others to attend. Ambassador Guo gave a speech on the spot to express his gratitude to the British cabinet members for their presence and the friendly assistance given to the two Chinese inspection groups. The two inspection groups conducted inspections in the UK more thoroughly than in any other country, which proves China's friendship and trust in the UK, and the UK is also eager to reciprocate. The recent speeches in the British newspapers and Parliament can prove that the British government and the public are now closely watching the current situation in China and understanding it more and more. He is gratified by this. Twelve years ago, British and American politicians cooperated in Washington, making the treaty have the power of understanding that a strong and unified China is the best guarantee for peace and prosperity in the Far East. At a time when the whole world needs a fair market more than ever before, the Chinese government is actively implementing construction plans and expanding its governance within the country. What China and the world need most now is a reaffirmation of the two major principles enshrined in the Nine-Power Treaty: the inviolability of China's territorial integrity and equal opportunities for all countries to trade in China. It is time for British and American politicians to take the lead in sponsoring the principles established in Washington in 1922, etc.

British Army Minister Hailsham delivered a very friendly and sympathetic reply after Ambassador Guo's speech, but did not involve the diplomatic events mentioned by Ambassador Guo. The Army Minister said that he admired the work of the Chinese government and was honored to meet with members of the two Chinese inspection groups. He hoped that they would get everything they wanted. (Reuters, 11th)

China's Silver Shipments to the US Not Reduced After Tax Collection

Half of the Total US Imports Last Month

(Washington) According to a report released by the Ministry of Commerce today, China is still the largest source of silver purchased by the United States in November. Although China levies an export tax on silver, the fact is that silver imported from China by the United States still accounts for more than half. The total value of silver purchased by the United States in November was US$15,010,561, of which US$7,576,401 was supplied by China, followed by the United Kingdom with US$4,137,457, and then Mexico with US$2,151,551. The total amount of silver imported by the United States in October was US$14,424,634, an increase of US$585,927 this month. Cash imports in November were US$121,198,645, an increase of US$108,189,136 compared to last month, most of which came from France, accounting for US$70,350,887, followed by Belgium with US$12,813,6585, Holland US$9,000,000, Canada US$9,000,000. The total export amount was US$309,659, compared to US$2,172,824 in October. (National Telegraph, 10th)

China Recovers Pilotage Rights

Britain and the United States Expected to Compromise

Japan Opposes Alone

(Tokyo) The Chinese government has recently been actively carrying out the movement to recover pilotage rights and has started negotiations with various countries including Britain, Japan, France, and Italy. Britain and the United States intend to compromise with China on the condition of protecting the livelihoods of their own pilots. However, Japan fears that China's recovery of pilotage rights from extraterritorial rights is not only a major issue in foreign policy, but also that its vested interests in national defense may be infringed upon. It strongly opposes it. The Ministry of Communications is scheduled to convene representatives of various shipping companies and people related to pilotage rights on the Yangtze River to solicit opinions and consider countermeasures. (Japan United Press, 11th)

British Naval, Land, and Air Forces

Joint Military Exercise in Singapore

Unprecedented in Scope

Naval Base Used for the First Time

Singapore: The British naval and land forces here are scheduled to begin joint military exercises on Thursday, which are quite extensive in nature and unprecedented here. There are currently 18 destroyers and 2 other warships here. Since the announcement of the military exercise, all sectors have paid close attention to this matter, because not only the naval, land, and air forces will participate, but the volunteer army will also participate in this exercise. The navy is responsible for the offensive, and various strategic locations in Singapore, including the naval base, will be the target of the navy's attack. The defenders are the regular army, air force, and volunteer army. The situation of the military exercise is not secret at all, and the general methods have long been known to everyone. However, both the attacking and defending sides naturally do not want to announce their detailed strategies. After the military exercise is completed, a press release will be issued at the front to announce everything. There are two points that people here are most concerned about: 1. This is the first opportunity to test the defense engineering of the naval base; 2. The Singapore volunteer army is an army that has not experienced war, and will now jointly resist the enemy with the regular army. (Reuters, 11th) Singapore: The Singapore naval base was used for the first time today by 16 destroyers. The ships will participate in the joint military exercise of the land, sea, and air forces that will begin on Thursday. It is learned that everything about this exercise will be kept strictly confidential. The rumor that it will be made public is not true. From October 13th to 16th, this port will be closed from a certain time to a certain time. The ships will not turn on their lights during night exercises. (Reuters, 11th)

London Talks Stalled

(Washington) According to reliable sources today, government officials have very little hope for holding a naval conference next year. This observation is the result of the London talks becoming deadlocked. If Japan abolishes the Washington and London Naval Treaties, the US delegation will regard it as a sign that the talks have completely ended. It is learned that the United States is still waiting for the Japanese representatives to take any action to avoid withdrawing when there is still a glimmer of hope. The US representatives hope that Japan can take formal action so that they can all return home and reunite with their families for the Christmas holidays. According to the most optimistic opinions in Washington officialdom, Japan can initiate another conference or implement a period of cooperation within the two-year period before the treaty expires. Otherwise, people generally believe that the United Kingdom and the United States will conclude an agreement to notify each other when building ships or to contact each other in other ways. Japan may also join this agreement. Although Washington officialdom and the national media have expressed their intention to compete with Japan in shipbuilding to maintain the existing naval ratio, they still hope that Japan can exercise self-restraint. (National Telegraph, 10th)

Japanese Privy Council

Passes the Draft to Abolish the Naval Treaty

Palace Conference to Be Held Again on the 19th

(Tokyo) The deliberation on the notification to abolish the Washington Naval Treaty was completed by the review committee of the Privy Council at 5:40 pm after questioning the government. Therefore, the government's committee members were asked to withdraw, and only the Privy Council discussed its attitude. At 6:20 pm, the draft to abolish the treaty was unanimously approved according to the government's original plan, and the meeting was adjourned. Chairman Pingzhan of the review committee and Chief Secretary Murakami made a review report, which was scheduled to be convened at the palace at 10 am on the 19th for a regular meeting to review it again for adoption. It has been confirmed that the government's original plan will be unanimously approved by the whole meeting. (Japan United Press, 11th)

Saito Declares Japan Does Not Fear Fighting Britain and the United States

Then Corrects His Words

Philadelphia: Japanese Ambassador Saito gave a speech here today, reiterating that Japan's main fleet cannot be lower than that of the United States. After the speech, Saito made a statement to the evening newspaper, saying that Japan will take the policies it deems necessary for the sake of establishing peace in the Far East. The intentions of Britain and the United States are not a concern. Even if it has to fight with the two countries, it will not hesitate. If Japan believes it is necessary to maintain peace in the Far East, it will also annex northern China, regardless of what other countries say or do. If the United States believes that Japan will become an imperialist country and wants to stop it, it should send a fleet to the Far East. But Japan is not an imperialist, and its intention is only to strictly maintain the existing treaties, especially the treaties on the open door in China, etc. (Havas, 10th)

(Washington) Ambassador Saito's meeting with a reporter from the American Bretton Evening News has caused a major reaction across the country because the newspaper is an upper-class newspaper in the United States. However, the interview as reported in the paper completely misinterpreted what was said, so the ambassador issued a statement on the night of the 10th denying it. The explanation is as follows: The reporter from the Bretton Evening News completely misunderstood what I said. What I said was that the United Kingdom and the United States will eventually understand Japan's policy. If the United Kingdom and the United States never understand no matter what, and unreasonably turn back the path taken by Japan, then Japan will have no choice but to go to war with them, etc. This is completely different from [even if it is unavoidable to fight with the United Kingdom and the United States, the plan in the Far East must still be implemented]. When the reporter asked me, he said, [If you go to war with the United Kingdom and the United States, Japan will definitely be defeated. Wouldn't the end result be national suicide?] I replied that the end result may be like this, but Japan is still working hard to achieve peace. Japan does not want to become an imperialist country, and of course does not have the idea of invading other countries. What Japan hopes for is peace and order in the Far East, etc. (Japan United Press, 10th)

British House of Commons Debates Indian Issues

Secretary of State for India Moves Motion

Requesting Acceptance of the Constitutional Reform Plan

(London) Secretary of State for India Hoare moved a government motion in the House of Commons this afternoon, not only accepting the recommendations of the Joint Select Committee on Indian Constitutional Reform, but also advocating the introduction of the Indian Constitution Bill based on the outline of the committee's report. The House of Commons then began debating, which is expected to last for three days. On Wednesday, the last day of the House of Commons debate, the Labour Party will introduce an amendment, advocating that the report should stipulate that legislation recognizes India's right to be upgraded to the status of an overseas self-governing territory, stipulate the gradual development and expansion of responsible government in India in order to reach the status of an overseas self-governing territory, and stipulate that India has the possibility of seeking political power through constitutional procedures. On Tuesday night, the last speaker on behalf of the government will be Privy Councillor Baldwin. It is expected that the government will get a majority of votes when this motion is put to a vote. After the House of Commons debate is over, the House of Lords will also discuss the case, which will also take about three days and end on December 18. Unless there is a need to reconvene a special congress of the Conservative Party in January, this parliamentary discussion will be the final stage of the discussion on the Indian Constitution by the parliament and non-parliament. After that, the government can introduce the Indian Constitution Bill, which contains about 300 articles, all of which are about the progressive measures on the Indian Constitution. It is expected that the discussion of the details of this case and its final passage will occupy most of the parliament's time in 1935. When the House of Commons began debating Secretary of State for India Hoare's motion today, the meeting was packed. Hoare spoke and asked the House of Commons to accept the recommendations of the Joint Select Committee, and said that the government is considering the report of the Joint Select Committee based on the proposal to support India and make it always a part of the British Empire. Indian public figures have long heard the teachings of using the Westminster Constitution as a model to engage in work. Indian social problems must be handled by responsible Indian politicians to be effective. This situation is becoming more and more obvious now. He does not want to make optimistic remarks hastily. In the future, he may encounter irreversible difficulties and suffer many disappointments. But he believes that the new constitution may develop along a very unique outline, rather than following the Westminster model. He is convinced that if a case is passed according to the outline of the Joint Select Committee report, then this constitution can be handled. The Indian National Congress has won a great victory in the recent parliamentary elections, which he does not regard as a strange thing. He knew early on that the National Congress would win many seats. For several years, the Indian Governor and he have had a certain policy to make the National Congress break away from the desolate situation of non-cooperation and join the responsible public work in the parliament. If a system that must rely on criticizing the government to succeed still exists, then the result of the Indian election will ultimately be like this. This is the lesson learned from this election. The measures to improve the Indian Constitution are proposed based on its advantages, and not because of weakness and timidity, we have to give in. We propose improvement measures only because we are convinced that it can improve Indian politics and make India a satisfactory member of the British Empire and British cooperation. The Labour Party's Attlee, on behalf of the opposition party, criticized this report for not mentioning India's goal of achieving the status of an overseas self-governing territory, saying that the Labour Party wants to see a constitution that can enable the Indian people to break away from social and economic evils. After 150 years of being ruled by the United Kingdom, the Indian people realize that they are still poor and ignorant. The British are slow to give responsibility to India, which is the fault of the British, and makes the benefits that the British have given to India offset. We must know that the idea that white people must rule the Indians for their own good is the psychology of the Victorian era and is no longer appropriate. The Liberal Party's Foot succeeded in speaking and supported the government's motion. Several Conservative Party members also spoke in succession, some supporting and some opposing this case. Finally, Attorney General Somervell rose to end today's debate and explained the federal issue. At this point, the meeting was adjourned until tomorrow for further debate. (Reuters, 10th)

Hires Women to Spy on Military Information

The Agricultural, Forestry, and Animal Husbandry Conditions in the Three Provinces

The Shanghai Municipal Government considers the publishing industry as a cultural institution, and the industry association has requested a reduction. It has been specially reduced. The Yuan handed it over to the Ministry of Finance for verification. (Special Telegram, 11th)

Shanghai Stock Exchange Prohibits Trading of Its Own Stocks

(Nanjing) Because the Shanghai Stock Exchange traded its own stocks in the market, causing a craze and disrupting finance, the Ministry of Finance specially ordered the supervisors of the stock exchange yesterday to transfer the order to the gold industry and securities exchanges to strictly ban trading to avoid causing malpractices. (Special Telegram, 11th)

Achievements in the Capital's Anti-Smoking Campaign

(Nanjing) Wang Zuxiang, Director of the Nanjing Municipal Health Bureau, stated that the capital has a firm determination to implement the anti-smoking campaign. It is expected to completely eradicate smoking within the stipulated time limit. The bureau's anti-smoking report for this year, from February 5th to the end of October, shows that a total of 2,150 smokers have quit smoking. Among them, 482 smokers quit voluntarily, while 1,886 smokers were forced to quit by the courts and other government agencies. (Eleventh Dispatch)

Korean Vagrants Selling Drugs in Ji-Mi District

(Beiping) According to a person from Ji County, Koreans in various counties of the Ji-Mi District are selling drugs under the guise of opening foreign firms for business. Though severely suppressed and investigated multiple times, they have gradually disappeared. However, recent investigations reveal that a small number of vagrants in Zunhua, Yutian, Sanhe, Huairou, and Ji County are secretly organizing drug-selling agencies. The local governments are paying close attention. (Eleventh Dispatch)

To date, the Japanese population in Japanese-controlled territories in the Northeast has reached 300,000, compared to 200,000 before the incident. Zhao Dazhong's Party Secretly Active

(Tianjin) The traitor Zhao Dazhong arrived in Tangshan on the 9th, stayed overnight, and went to Shanhaiguan on the 10th. Zhao's whereabouts are very secretive. His party member, Guo Lantian, is currently acting on Zhao's orders and is still active in the four eastern mines of Kailuan. On the 11th, police officers from the Tianjin Public Security Bureau arrested a man on the border between the eastern suburbs of the city and the county. The man was carrying 15 wooden fake seals of various sizes with blank certificates. The seals all bore the characters of a fake military unit, and the certificates contained similar wording. After being detained by the bureau for interrogation, he firmly refused to confess, only claiming that he found them on the road. (Eleventh Dispatch)

Customs Officers at Yuguan Seize Medicinal Materials

A detachment of foreign military police and the Shanhaiguan garrison both lodged protests, demanding the full return of the goods. (Eleventh Dispatch)

Hebei Construction Department Requests Funds for Flood Control

(Tianjin) The Hebei Construction Department received a telegram from the Yellow River Conservancy Bureau stating that the Yellow River ice flood has arrived. Several breaches in the embankment have not been completed, and many of the levees are old and dilapidated. Urgent measures are needed to strengthen defenses, otherwise, the levees may collapse when the ice arrives. They are currently supervising workers to strengthen the protection and request the speedy allocation of flood control funds for application. The department has requested the Finance Department to quickly allocate 2,900 yuan for emergency use. (Eleventh Dispatch)

Social Depression in Cities and Towns of War Zone

(Tianjin) In cities and towns of the war zone, social depression is rampant, and the countryside is bankrupt. Local products from the four eastern provinces cannot be transported and sold outside the customs, leading to an increasing number of unemployed people. On the 9th, when the Qinhuangdao Customs Bureau recruited 11 guards, there were over a thousand applicants. Teachers and students from the Tian Family Middle School in Yuguan traveled dozens of miles in a group of over a hundred people. (Eleventh Dispatch)

New Poisonous Agent Discovered in Luandong

(Tianjin) Due to the impact of our anti-drug campaign on the sales of heroin, a certain foreign national has recently invented a poisonous agent called "Sweet Pill." It is made of heroin, morphine, and saccharin, shaped like a candy ball. It dissolves in the mouth, taking effect after one minute. It is divided into 2-yuan, 1-yuan, and 2-jiao/3-jiao versions. After consumption, it is impossible to quit. If one does not consume it, addiction symptoms occur with severe abdominal pain. Consuming it for one year leads to the poison penetrating the bone marrow and death. Currently, sales are booming in various parts of Tangdong. Unknowing people, because of its cheapness and convenience, are fond of consuming it. Consumers in Yutian and Luan County are particularly numerous. A certain foreign national has set up an agency in Changli County, specializing in sales and manufacturing. (Eleventh Dispatch)

New Accounting System to Be Implemented in Various Counties North of the Yangtze

(Zhenjiang) The meeting of accounting directors from various counties north of the Yangtze River convened by the Jiangsu Finance Department has concluded. The key points instructed are: 1. Gold and Silver

▲English Gold: London gold price, today's listing is 140 shillings 4.5 pence, the same as yesterday's price.

▲English Silver: London silver market this morning, the market opened at 375, spot price is 24 pence 625, futures is 24 pence 75. Speculators bought, China bought and then sold, the market situation is stable.

▲American Silver: Mount Lyell silver market, opening price is higher.

Exchange Rates

▲British-American: London foreign exchange market, trading was sparse this morning. The opening exchange rate for British pounds to US dollars was 4 dollars, 9 jiao, 5 fen, 125, which is 625 lower than yesterday. There was a slight fluctuation later. The latest price is 4 dollars, 9 jiao, 5 fen, 3125.

▲British-French: The opening was 75 francs, 12, which is 9 pounds lower than yesterday. Then it fell another 6 pounds. At noon, it rose 3 pounds to 75 francs 09. This is the market price at the time of the telegram.

▲American-British: New York foreign exchange market, the opening price for US dollars to British pounds was 4 dollars, 9 jiao, 5 fen, 25, which is half a cent lower. The exchange rate between US dollars and French francs remained unchanged at 6 dollars, 5 jiao, 9 fen, 25.

Cotton and Wheat

▲American Cotton: The cotton market is narrow. Due to rumors of continuous sales of stockpiled cotton, buyers are hesitant to advance. Rubber

Yu Xuezhong Discusses the Difficulties of Provincial and Municipal Boundary Demarcation

The Provincial Government Believes There Is Fundamentally No New Boundary to Demarcate

Otherwise, the County Governance Would Face the Issue of Existence or Abolition

Beiping Correspondence: Hebei Chairman Yu Xuezhong arrived in Beiping from Tianjin yesterday (7th) at 6:40 PM. After getting off the train, he returned to his private residence to rest. On the 8th, he visited Huang Fu and returned to Tianjin in the evening. According to Yu, [This trip was to visit Huang to report on the situation after the reorganization of the Provincial Government. Although the relocation of the Provincial Government to Baoding has been approved by the Central Government, the actual date of relocation has not yet been determined. The joint office operations of the Provincial Government and the establishment of departments in various counties will be implemented on New Year's Day next year. It is currently being actively prepared. The Beiping-Hebei boundary demarcation conference began in Nanjing on the 8th. The Hebei Provincial Government representatives Zhang Lisheng, Hu Yuanhui, Zhang Yinwu, and others have been appointed and have already gone to Nanjing. The Provincial Government's opinion on boundary demarcation is the same as the resolution of the first meeting of the Hebei Provincial Government some time ago: the previously defined area should be the scope of boundary demarcation. Tianjin reported that Zhao Dazhong went to Tangshan again, but the report received by the Provincial Government was that Zhao had previously gone to Suizhong. It is not yet known whether he is now in Tangshan] and so on.

Another report states that when Yu Xuezhong visited Huang Fu at 4 PM today (8th), he reported in detail on the reorganization of the Hebei Provincial Government and the appointment of new officials. He left around 5 PM. Yu also said today that [Regarding the issue of Beiping-Hebei boundary demarcation, some parties still believe that the provincial and municipal boundaries are to be redrawn. After the reorganization of the Hebei Provincial Government, the first meeting resolved that the boundary demarcation should be based on the original boundaries. The Provincial Government believes that there is fundamentally no new boundary to demarcate, because each county has a defined boundary. Once it is divided, the county that is drastically reduced will face the issue of existence or abolition. This morning, I read in the newspaper that Nanjing may only劃割大小汤山 and Nanyuan into Beiping. In this regard, Tangshan is within the boundary of Changping County, which is more than 40 li away from Beiping. If Tangshan is taken, who is responsible for those 40 li between Tangshan and Beiping? If that stretch is included as well, Changping will have lost so much territory that the point of its existence will be questioned. So I say that this matter cannot be decided until detailed discussion has occurred. And in the final decision, the Provincial Government will only listen to the orders of the Central Government. Because it is now winter, it is cold, and the end of the year is approaching, whether the relocation of the Provincial Government to Baoding can be completed and implemented before the new year has not yet been determined. (8th)

Fellow Countrymen from Northeast and Shandong Return to Their Hometowns

Due to the Difficulty of Making a Living, They Are Returning to Shandong in Succession

Over Two Thousand People Have Returned in Recent Days

Jinan Correspondence: The four northeastern provinces have been occupied by the Japanese military for three years. All interests and treasures have been exploited by the Japanese. This has led to economic stagnation and rural bankruptcy. The level of living has increased by a fold compared to the past. The fellow countrymen from Shandong who went outside the customs previously saved 50 or 100 yuan and sent it back to Shandong every year, but now due to the rise in the price of food such as sorghum and soybeans, the income is still the same as before, without any increase. Those with high incomes can only barely maintain their livelihood, and those with less income feel very inadequate. Moreover, it is now winter and approaching the end of the year. In recent days, all fellow countrymen from Shandong have returned to Shandong in succession. One route is to take the puppet Fengshan road to enter the customs and return to Shandong along the Jinpu Railway, and the other route is to take Dalian and take the sea route to Qingdao, and then return to their original hometown along the Jiaoji Line. Every day, there are as many as a thousand people and at least several hundred people. They are all returning to Shandong because they cannot bear the Japanese abuse and can only barely collect about 20 yuan of travel expenses. (9th)

Communist Bandits in Northern Guangxi Flee to Western Hunan

Guangxi Troops Sent to Help Defend Eastern Guizhou

Guangzhou Correspondence: The Communist bandits Zhu De, Peng Dehuai, Lin Biao, and Dong Litang, who fled to northern Guangxi, were very rampant when they arrived in Wenshi. After the Guangxi army concentrated its forces and launched attacks from Xinwei, Gulingtou, and other places, the Communist bandits suffered heavy casualties in the battles of Wenshi and Shitang. The Communist bandits had no intention of fighting and broke through the Quanzhou-Xing'an line, extending westward to western Hunan. Kong divided up a detachment to go south along Quanzhou, Guishan, and Zaojieshou, to constrain the Guangxi army to encircle from Guilin, in order to cover the fleeing bandits into western Hunan. Since the 2nd of this month, they have successively occupied the line from Xianshui to the west to Lutang and Luojiang. The main force fled to Meixi. The deputy commander of the Guangxi army, Bai Chongxi, is in charge of directing the armies to pursue and suppress them. He set off from Pingle to Xing'an at 3 PM on the afternoon of the 2nd to instruct the armies on the strategy of pursuit and suppression. At the same time, in order to assist the Guizhou army in blocking the attack, in addition to sending the 15th Army to track down and pursue the bandits, he also sent the 7th Army to bypass Guizhou to assist the Guizhou army and consolidate border defenses. The telegram from Bai received here roughly stated: (1) The bandits from Shitangxu, Mazidu, and Fuhuapu were defeated by our army at 4 PM yesterday (1st), and a full-scale pursuit began. Since this morning, the battlefield has been continuously cleared, and the advance has been made to the line of Lutang, west of Xianshui. The bandits fled to the roads to Tongmei and Xikou. I will transfer to Xing'an at 3 PM this afternoon (2nd) to handle the subsequent pursuit. (2) It is certain that the bandits who fought with our army this time are the main force of the pseudo-135th Army Group, numbering over 20,000. The remaining bandits fled from the road from Xianshui to the Mei Creek Estuary, and from the Che Tian to the Long Sheng Jiang Road from Yan (29th) onwards. According to the combined information from all parties, it is judged that the bandits still have at least 50,000 to 60,000 people. (3) In addition to the 15th Army tracking down and pursuing the bandits, the 7th Army will bypass the border between Guangxi and Guizhou to assist friendly forces in blocking. (4) In the five days of fighting with the bandits in the Xingquan border area, a total of over 1,000 bandits were killed, over 2,000 were captured, and there were 500 Guangxi bandits who originally belonged to Li Mingrui, who surrendered, and 5,200 guns were seized. Furthermore, among the captured bandits, in addition to those from this province who are intended to stay in Guangxi or be sent elsewhere, there are over 2,000 from various provinces, but mostly from Jiangxi and Hunan, and there are officials of all levels among them. Should they be sent to the Central Government, or should they be handed over to Brother Yun? (Note: i.e., He Jian) A telegraphic instruction is awaited. Chongxi Dong (2) sent a seal, etc. Yesterday another telegram was received, stating that the entire Guangxi 7th and 15th armies contacted the bandits' 13th Army Group in Jieshou on the 3rd. The bandits fought and retreated, and they will be unsupported. (5th)

Anhui Province Loan Contract Signed

Five Banks Start Paying the Funds

Wuhu Correspondence: Due to the severe drought in Anhui Province this year, the tax revenue has been sharply reduced. With the end of the year approaching, there are no administrative expenses to pay. Last month, the Provincial Government sent Finance Director Mao Longcao to Shanghai to borrow 800,000 yuan from five banks: Shanghai, Central, China, Jiaotong, and Shanghai Industrial Bank. Together with the 400,000 yuan previously promised by the Wuhu branch of each bank, the total is 1.2 million yuan, with the surplus of the salt revenue that Anhui Province should receive as collateral. After the arrangements were agreed upon, Mao took the draft contract back to Anhui and submitted it to the Provincial Government meeting for discussion. The original arrangements and draft contract were approved and sent to Li Shiqian, director of the Wuhu office, to be responsible for handling the liaison. After receiving the order, Director Li immediately began to contact the five branches of the Central Bank, etc. At the same time, the five branches also received a telegram from the Shanghai head office, notifying them of the results of the loan negotiations and ordering them to implement them in accordance with the agreed-upon arrangements. After several contacts between the two parties, all procedures have been completed. The Anhui Salt Affairs Inspection Office also submitted to the General Office for approval to use the 193,000 yuan monthly surplus of the Anhui Province collaboration as collateral. Therefore, the formal loan contract was signed at the Wuhu branch of the Central Bank today. At this point, the Anhui Province loan issue was completely settled. The amount of the loan undertaken by the five banks is 600,000 yuan from the Central Bank and a total of 600,000 yuan from the four banks of China, Jiaotong, Shanghai, and Shanghai Industrial Bank, making up the total of 1.2 million. Since the contract has been signed and the procedures have been arranged, the five branches have decided to pay 400,000 yuan first on the 15th of this month, another 400,000 yuan at the end of the year, and the remaining 3 to 400,000 yuan will be paid 200,000 yuan each on February 1st and June 1st next year. The loan stipulates a monthly interest rate of 8%, and starting from February next year, over 70,000 yuan will be withdrawn from the monthly surplus of 193,000 yuan in salt revenue to be repaid, and the full amount will be repaid in 20 months. With this large sum of money, the Anhui Provincial Government may be able to pass the end of this year safely. (10th)

Repeated Seizure of Counterfeit Organizations of the East River in Guangdong Province

Defection of the Pseudo-East River Guerrilla Leader

Guiding Military Police to Crack Down on Pseudo-Organizations

Shantou Correspondence: Gu Dacun's remnant bandit group in the eastern district of Guangdong Province was encircled and suppressed by Zhang Ruigui's division in Nanshan in previous years. The operation lasted more than a year, and most of the bandits were wiped out. Gu led more than a thousand bandits to flee back to Tongziyang in Baxiang Mountain, Fengshun County. This spring, Deng Longguang's division again suppressed them, directing the police guards of various counties to cooperate in the suppression. The remnant bandits of Gu's forces had very few remaining members. Among them, Deng Caiping, the leader of the pseudo-East River guerrilla brigade, with dozens of followers, scattered into Jiulongzhang, Hanxi, Douxi, Yangqiankeng, and other areas at the intersection of Mei and Feng counties. Under the surveillance of the police and civilian militias of various districts and townships, they were unable to survive. Two months ago, they fled back into the Tongziyang mountains, building two thatched shelters to prepare for the winter. Upon receiving this information, He Yinghua's troops, the first battalion of the Second Regiment of the Independent Second Division of the Fengshun garrison, immediately joined forces with the civilian militias of various districts and townships to search and suppress them day and night. At that time, the bandits had nowhere to escape. On November 30th, Deng Caiping personally carried a Mauser pistol and hand grenades and surrendered to He's battalion, requesting permission to atone for his crimes through meritorious service. That very night, he guided the military police to crack down on the general headquarters of the Communist Party's Fengjie District Working Committee, killing Hu Gen, the pseudo-chairman and military commander, and two other key bandits. They captured five key East River bandits, seized two short guns, and a large quantity of reactionary propaganda. In recent days, due to Deng Caiping's defection, the East River communists knew that they could no longer hide and live in peace, and they also surrendered one after another. Wang Minduo, the commander of the third battalion, has been dispatched to Heshidun and other places in the third district of Fengshun in recent days to inspect defenses and rectify military discipline. He also cracked down on a communist organization in Changkeng Township, capturing key bandits Li Zima, Li Jinlu, female bandit Luo Meilu, and others on the spot, seizing several long guns. Li Zima then led the team to Dakeng Township, Jieyang County, to encircle and suppress the communists. The bandits fled upon hearing the news, and only the organization was destroyed. Battalion Commander Wang executed eleven important communists by firing squad a few days ago, including Peng Xinmin and Peng Daoming, members of the pseudo-Soviet executive committee of the Dabu-Fengshun district, Huang Teng, bandit soldier Cai Suixiang, Yang Miaojin, Zhang A Yuan, Zhang A Ding, members of the pseudo-Soviet executive committee of the Pailing district of Wuhua, as well as key bandits Chen Kang, Chen Weihua, Li Jinlu of Changkeng Township, female bandit department head Luo Meilu, and others, who were executed on the spot at the Tangkeng regimental headquarters. The East River communists can now be expected to be eradicated. (4th)

The Various Counties of Anhui Province Continue to Undertake the Fourth Phase of Water Conservancy Projects

| A Period of Eight Months |

Anqing Correspondence: Under the supervision of the Construction Department of Anhui Province, the various counties of the province have been undertaking water conservancy projects in phases since the previous year. As of the end of May this year, three phases have been completed, with notable success in addressing the symptoms of flood and drought prevention. The eight-month period from October 22 to May 23 was particularly effective. A total of over 2.4 million zhang of dikes were repaired, over 12.2 million fang of earth were built, and over 700,000 zhang of ditches and rivers were dredged, with over 5.4 million fang of earth removed. Over 30 ponds were repaired, increasing the volume by over 900,000 fang. The total amount of earthwork completed was over 18.5 million fang, or over 68.45 million cubic meters. From October 23 to the end of May 24, the fourth phase of water conservancy projects will be undertaken for eight months. The provincial government has been requested to follow the precedents of the previous three phases, instructing the governments of the 60 counties to formulate implementation plans for the fourth phase of water conservancy projects based on the needs of each county and in accordance with local conditions. After approval, the construction sites and methods will be listed, and report forms will be filled out and submitted accordingly. Construction will be carried out immediately so that personnel can be dispatched at any time for inspection and acceptance. Currently, the counties that have submitted the plans include Fuyang, Yingshang, Huoqiu, Hao County, Mengcheng, Taihe, Woyang, Fengyang, Huaiyuan, Lingbi, Su County, Dingyuan, Shou County, Si County, Wuhe, Tianchang, Jiashan, Chu County, Lai An, Quanjiao, Hefei, Shucheng, Wuwei, Lujiang, Chao County, He County, Hanshan, Wuhu, Dangtu, Fanchang, Guichi, Qingyang, Tongling, Shidai, Dongji, Huaining, Tongcheng, Qianshan, Taihu, Wangjiang, Xuancheng, Nanling, Ningguo, Jingde, Taiping, Guangde, Langxi, She County, Xiuning, Yi County, and Jixi, a total of 51 counties. The submitted plans are generally well-organized and practical for implementation. They are currently being reviewed and instructed to commence construction immediately. (9th)

Songjiang: Water Patrol Team Captures Two Thieves

Feng Zhaolin, a villager from the 16th and 17th villages of the Punan Caojing District, was robbed on the night of the 8th of this month, losing 17 silver dollars, 12,000 copper coins, and silver ornaments. He immediately reported the incident to Fei Gongxia of the Songjiang County (Song Feng boundary) Water Patrol Team stationed in Kulin Town, who, along with squad leaders Xia Shutang and Li Qiu, rushed to arrest the thieves. On the night of the 9th, they captured the thieves Zhang Yunsheng (36 years old) and Zhang Jinrong (32 years old) in the Hongmiao area, and seized stolen goods such as silver bracelets. After interrogation, they confessed to the robbery without denying it. The victim was called to identify the stolen goods as his. On the 11th, they were escorted to the county government for interrogation.

Suzhou

Zhirou Boxing Association Resumes the Suzhou Branch: The Zhirou Boxing Association established a branch in Suzhou in the 18th year of the Republic, which lasted for two years, achieving significant results. Affected by the January 28th Incident, it was suspended. Now, the president of the association, Chen Weiming, has gone to Suzhou to resume the branch. The address is inside the Chide Hospital on Zhangguang Bridge. The people of Suzhou will surely be eager to join.

Qingpu

Fire in Lijing Village Injures People

Lijing Village, outside the south gate of this town, has more than 20 households, all of whom are farmers. During this harvest season, all the rice is stored in the fields. Yesterday, at around 11 a.m., thick smoke and flames suddenly erupted from the top of Chen Heming's rice stack. By the time it was discovered and the villagers went to rescue it, the rice stacks of neighboring Ren Shaomei and Shou Shenglong had also been affected. Although the villagers tried their best to put out the fire, the flames were too strong and spread rapidly. Several large trees in the field were also burned down. By the time Yang Long from the Chengnan District came to help put out the fire, about 70% of the more than 300 mu of rice stacks had been burned. One strong man was injured by a fall, and one child was burned. The total loss is estimated to be over 5,000 yuan.

Wuxi

Modern Girl Attempts Suicide in Hotel

A woman from Liyang, around 28 years old, fashionably dressed and charming, checked into the Washington Hotel on Guangqin Road on the 6th of this month, claiming to be named Wang Lanying. She booked room 21 and stayed for several nights. She was visited by several male friends. The night before last, around 9 p.m., the woman called her boyfriend Liu Guangping and expressed her worries, looking sad and tearful. Later, around 10 p.m., she suddenly swallowed one yuan worth of raw opium and attempted suicide. After taking the opium, she sobbed softly in the room. She then tried to go out alone, but the tea waiter noticed something was wrong. At that time, Liu Guangping also arrived with several people. Seeing the situation, they took her to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. Fortunately, she was not severely poisoned and was saved. According to the woman, she attempted suicide because she was unable to pursue her studies. However, her words and behavior were very strange.

Land Price Declaration Deadline Will Not Be Extended

The Urban Land Price Declaration Office held a meeting with the township officials yesterday. First, Hu Pin Fang, director of the Land Bureau, reported that the 15-day extension period for land price declarations is about to expire, with only five days remaining. Within these five days, all officials must intensify their work to complete the task as scheduled. All declaration forms issued must be collected by the 15th of this month and submitted to the office for review in order to be announced and registered. It should be known that this extension is a special concession from the government. After the deadline, no further extensions will be granted. Landowners who conceal their land and fail to report it will be dealt with in accordance with Article 7 of the provincial urban land price declaration regulations. Currently, the number of declaration forms received by the officials and those submitted in person by the owners at the office account for about 60% of the total. It is expected that all declaration forms will be completed before the 15th.

Funding Secured for Dredging Rivers

Zhang Fulin, the director of the Construction Bureau of this county, previously received instructions from the Construction Department to organize labor relief to dredge the rivers throughout the county. After dispatching personnel to selectively measure the rivers, the following rivers have been measured for dredging: Yongxing River, Beixingtang River, Panshu Port, Xiantang River, Sitou River, Zhangjingqiao River, Yujiaqiao River, Nanmali Port, Yangshuyuan River, Lujiangkou, Lijian River, Changguangxi, Renzigang, and Liangzang River, etc. The required funding is estimated to be 100,000 yuan. A detailed plan and budget have been submitted to the Construction Department for approval and appropriation of funds to facilitate the project. After receiving the submission, Director Shen of the Construction Department stated that this year's river dredging will be carried out through labor relief. However, Wuxi has many rivers, and the construction funds are limited. Therefore, selective dredging is still necessary. A sum of 15,000 yuan has been approved, and the county must also raise 15,000 yuan, for a total of 30,000 yuan. A revised plan and budget should be submitted for review and approval. The Construction Bureau of this county was notified of this instruction yesterday. After receiving the order, Director Zhang consulted with County Magistrate Yan and planned to use 10,000 yuan from the construction water conservancy funds and 5,000 yuan from the public funds for repairing dikes in various districts. A construction discussion meeting will be convened within the next few days. Once approved, work can begin.

Nantong

District-Level Water and Land Bandit Prevention Measures

The counties of Tong, Ru, Chong, Hai, Jing, and Qi under the jurisdiction of Nantong District are now being instructed by the District Security Command to send teams to patrol on land, using the baojia system to investigate and suppress bandits. The bandit police in each county will suppress bandits without territorial restrictions. On the water, the water police team is responsible for defense deployment. Special water patrol teams have been formed at the coastal salt farms to take on defense duties. The county magistrates will immediately expel wandering soldiers and scattered bandits from their respective territories.

Yangzhou

Staff Officer of the Military Survey Unit Beaten

The land declaration in this county is progressing smoothly. On the 9th, a military survey team from the Army Survey Unit of the General Staff Headquarters was surveying the fortress map in the Laozang area of the third district of the county. The local villagers mistakenly believed that the survey had started immediately after the land declaration, which they considered inconsistent with the government orders. They gathered and beat the surveyors, destroying the survey instruments. Upon receiving the news, the county government sent the injured personnel to the hospital for treatment and ordered Li Youguang, the superintendent of the Public Security Bureau, to rush to the scene on the 10th to suppress the incident. County Magistrate Ma also went to persuade them on the morning of the 11th to prevent the situation from escalating. It is reported that the county government has sent telegrams to the provincial government, requesting the General Staff Headquarters to suspend the survey during the land declaration period to complete the land policy.

Local News

Liu Wendao Set Sail for His Post Yesterday Morning

Over a Hundred Relatives and Friends Saw Him Off at the Wharf

Scheduled to Arrive in Italy on the 3rd of Next Month, to Visit the Prime Minister First

Liu Wendao, the newly appointed ambassador to Italy, along with his wife and children, as well as embassy staff member Liu Qian and a Western nanny, boarded the Italian mail ship Conte Verde at 11 a.m. yesterday to set off for Italy to assume his post. He is scheduled to arrive in Italy on the 3rd or 4th of next month. A large crowd of people saw him off at the wharf. The details are as follows:

Those Seeing Him Off

Representatives from the Hubei Fellow-Provincials Association in Shanghai, holding small flags that read "Congratulations to Ambassador Liu for Serving the Party and the Country," as well as over sixty teachers and students from libraries and schools, had been waiting at the New Customs Wharf since 8 a.m. Subsequently, people from all walks of life arrived to see him off, including Yu Hongjun, the Secretary-General representing Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Secretary Geng Jiaji, Lin Shiliang representing Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi, Secretary Wang Zhinan representing Yang Hu, the Director of the Shanghai Security Office, Zhao Tiezhang, the section chief of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Shanghai office, Madam Shi Meili, the wife of former Minister of Foreign Affairs Wang Zhengting, celebrity Huang Yanpei, former envoy to Switzerland Wu Kaisheng, former Director of General Affairs of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Fan Guang, Tang Zhaoshi, the secretary of the Jianghai Customs Superintendent's Office, Liu Wendao's younger brother Wenjie, Italian Ambassador to China Baoska Li, Consul General of Shanghai Nairong, and relatives and friends, totaling over a hundred people.

Departure Details

Mr. Liu, along with his wife and others, traveled by car from their residence on Shanzhong Road to the New Customs Wharf at 9:10 a.m. He then boarded the prepared Customs boat Jinghui with a group of people to see him off. At 9:45 a.m., they crossed to the Qichangzhan Wharf in Pudong and boarded the Italian ship. At that time, the Shanghai Security Office specially dispatched a company of security guards to line up alongside the ship for security, and a full military band was dispatched to play music. In addition, Mr. and Mrs. Wang Zhengting and Mr. and Mrs. Yang Hu each presented Mr. and Mrs. Liu with a flower basket. After saying goodbye to the people seeing him off in the ship's lounge, the ship left the port at exactly 11 a.m. amidst the melodious sound of military music.

Remarks Before Departure

When departing, Mr. Liu made a brief speech to the reporters at the wharf, saying that he expected to arrive in Venice, Italy, on the 3rd or 4th of next month, and then go to Rome, where he would first pay a visit to Prime Minister Mussolini, and then schedule an audience with the Italian Emperor to present his credentials. The friendly relations between China and Italy have always been very harmonious. In the future, he, Liu Wendao, will make every effort to further advance them. As for the domestic situation, he hopes that the Chinese people will strive to save themselves. The Grand Cordon of the Order of the Jade was presented by our National Government to the former Italian Ambassador to China, Count Ciano, etc., was taken by him to Italy, and after presenting his credentials in Rome, the capital of Italy, he will schedule a ceremony to present the awards on behalf of the National Government, and a grand ceremony will be held. It is also learned that Mr. Liu will return to China next year.

The Haili Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday

Two Students Studying in Belgium and Teng Shibiao Came Together

The third new ship, Haili, of the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, sailed from England to China on October 22. The previous night, it encountered fog 40 to 50 miles off the coast of Wusong. For safety, the shipowner reduced speed. It did not enter the Wusong estuary until 10:15 a.m. yesterday. At 1 p.m., it arrived at Gaochangmiao and immediately entered the third new dock of the Jiangnan Shipyard. It is scheduled to have the machinery inspected by the British shipyard and the Shanghai representative of the Markkang Company, together with the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company today. After the inspection is completed, it will be handed over to the Jiangnan Shipyard for painting and scheduled for acceptance.

Encountering Wind on the Way

A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency boarded the ship yesterday to meet with Teng Tubiao, the shipowner of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company who returned with the ship. According to him, the Haili was completed on October 20 and test-driven in England, which was deemed satisfactory. It then set sail for Shanghai that evening, passing through Gibraltar, Marseille, the Suez Canal, Aden, Colombo, Singapore, Little Luzon, and Xiamen before arriving in Shanghai. In Little Luzon, a hurricane passed through, so it stopped in Little Luzon for a day to avoid the wind. In the Fujian-Zhejiang waters, it encountered wind and fog, so it reduced speed, averaging only six nautical miles per hour. The ship's speed is 13.5 nautical miles per hour, so it arrived in Shanghai three days later than scheduled.

Personnel Coming Together

The Haili arrived in Shanghai yesterday with a total of 26 people, including the foreign shipowner, first mate, second mate, chief engineer, old engineer, second engineer, third engineer, radio operator, one each, two Chinese stewards, two chief cooks, four helmsmen, one stoker foreman, five stokers, one sailor foreman, and three sailors. In addition, there was Teng Shibiao, the shipowner of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and Wang Chengzuo and Zhou Yanqin, students from the Wusong Merchant Marine School who were previously sent to the British shipyard for practical training. In addition, there were our students studying in Belgium, one surnamed Feng and one surnamed Xu, who were introduced by our minister Guo Taiqi in England and returned with the ship, totaling 31 people.

Assigned Crew

At 4 p.m. yesterday, shipowner Teng Shibiao and trainees Zhou Yanqin and Wang Chengzuo went to the head office to report to Zhao Yuntai and Zhou Houkun, the chiefs of the shipping section, and Liu Hongsheng, the general manager. The bureau has assigned shipowner Teng Shibiao, first mate Chen Bangda, second mate Yang Biru, chief engineer Ni Shunlai, chief oiler Xu Wenxiang, second oiler Kong Xingui, steward Zhang Lisheng, sailor foreman Yan Peikang, and stoker foreman Shi Jincai. After acceptance, the ship will make its maiden voyage, which is planned to run on the Qingdao, Shanghai, Xiamen, Shantou, Hong Kong, and Guangzhou lines, and will also serve Wan and Lianyungang.

Wu Has Arrived in Shanghai

The Ministry of Communications previously sent Wu Daming and Shi Gan to England as supervisors for the construction of four ocean-going vessels. Now, the four vessels have been completed and sailed to Shanghai one after another. Wu Daming returned to Shanghai from England by ship and reported the supervision process to Liu Hongsheng, the general manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, the other day. He also went to Beijing the day before yesterday to report to Zhu Jiahua, the Minister of Communications. At the same time, he returned to his post as section chief of the Maritime Administration Department. As for Shi Gan, he has taken the fourth ship, the Haiyuan, to Shanghai and is expected to arrive in Shanghai before the end of this month.

Liu Weichi Talks About the Status of Preparing a Paper Mill

According to Liu Weichi, the vice minister of the Ministry of Industry, who was on the Yuebao ship on the morning of the 10th, the Ministry of Industry decided to set up a paper mill, in view of the fact that most of the various types of paper on the market came from abroad. The factory site has been surveyed and determined to be Wenzhou, Zhejiang. The capital is set at 6 million yuan, jointly run by the government and businessmen, with the government shares accounting for 4.8 million, which is being borrowed from the British Boxer Indemnity fund. This has been completely resolved, and the remaining 1.2 million yuan of commercial shares have also been determined. It could have been started immediately, but unfortunately, after the assassination of Shi Liangcai, the representative of the commercial shares, problems arose with the commercial shares. Therefore, the promotion of the factory must wait until the commercial share representatives are re-elected before it can continue.

All the staff of this newspaper held a memorial meeting for General Manager Shi Liangcai at the Hushe on the 8th of this month. The following is the reply telegram from Chairman Jiang: Mr. Zhang Yunhe and Mr. Ma Yinliang, I have received your telegram and have telegraphed the authorities in Zhejiang and Shanghai to step up the investigation and arrest within a time limit to take action. Jiang Zhongzheng, True Secret Jing, Print.
