(Shen Bao, Fourth Page)

Education News

Eleventh Day of the National Labor Exhibition

▲Judging Committee Holds Meeting and Decides on Judging Standards

▲More Than 2,000 Visitors Yesterday, Opening Today

(Nanjing, November 11th, Electric Dispatch) The Labor Exhibition Achievement Judging Committee held a meeting on the 11th at the Ministry of Education. Present were Gu Shusen, etc., six members of the Labor Exhibition Preparatory Committee, and Zhang Zhiwen, etc., fourteen judges. Chairman Gu reported on: 1. Judging assignments: For vocational work, agriculture was assigned to Zou Shu, Zhang Zhiwen; mechanics to Zhong Daozan; applied chemistry to Wei Yuanguang; dyeing and weaving to Liu Xunlin; civil engineering to Lu Enxu; commerce to Ding Yutian. For labor work, please assign Wei Dan, Shu He, Mingzhai Xiong, Zhu Gao, Ni Hua Sun, and Yi Qing Zhu, Su Nian, six people. To be responsible for embroidery and sewing, please assign Zhuang Zeyi. To be responsible for overall judgment on education, please assign Yang Zhensheng Zhuang Zeyi. 2. During unit review, first take the item as the unit, and later aggregate various items, calculate the total to produce school units and provincial/municipal units. 3. Handling of excellent products of labor: Excellent products of labor will be sent to the Educational Research Institute of Zhongda for display. Excellent vocational products will be sent to the Vocational Education Hall organized by the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau for display, and excellent products will be classified, photographed, and compiled into external volumes for school reference. Matters resolved: 1. Review procedure: divided into preliminary review and re-review. During the preliminary review, first select excellent products and mark them with a symbol. During the re-review, the reviewers will jointly review. 2. During the preliminary review of labor achievements, it was decided to use the method of branch review, and the allocation is as follows: First Hall, by Xiong Zhu, Gao Ni, Zhu Hua, Jiang Dan Shu; Second Hall and Third Hall by Sun Yiqing, He Mingqi, Liu Su Yu; 3. Judging standards: A. Must have educational significance. 1. Able to suit the level of students. 2. Must have labor training value. 3. Have a design plan. 4. Have a creative spirit. 5. Able to use scientific methods or principles. 6. Have national defense significance. B. Must have economic value. 1. Suitable for local needs. 2. Suitable for production conditions. 3. Suitable for living needs. 4. During judging, it is necessary to fully prepare the first, second, and third items of the standards. For the fourth, fifth, and sixth items of item A, and the first, second, and third items of item B, it is only necessary to have one item in each of the three items for judging. Symbols: use A, B, C. 4. A general comment must be recorded. 5. For the judging table style, please have Xiong Zhu Gao draft it.

On the 11th, the groups visiting the Labor Exhibition included the Children's School of Transportation Workers, totaling 2,396 people.

One of the products of Jiangsu Provincial Shanghai Middle School (Machine Made)

Written After the Closing of the Labor Exhibition by Huang Longxian

The unprecedented and sensational National Vocational School and Primary and Secondary School Labor Education Achievement Exhibition closed today. The preparation for the exhibition lasted several months. A total of 30 provinces and cities participated in the exhibition, with over 30,000 exhibits. The exhibition lasted for twelve days, and attracted tens of thousands of visitors. It was indeed a grand event. In recent years, there have been many exhibitions, such as individual art exhibitions of calligraphy, painting, seal engraving, and other arts, the West Lake Exposition, the National Railway Line Product Exhibition, the National Mining and Geological Exhibition, and the recently held National Vocational School and Primary and Secondary School Labor Education Achievement Exhibition. Individual art exhibitions are private in nature, while expositions like the Mining Exhibition and Labor Exhibition are organized by the government. The motivations are different, and the purposes are naturally different. Among the latter four, the Exposition and the Railway Exhibition are somewhat similar in nature. The Mining Exhibition belongs to a specialized field, and is not fully understood by the general public. The Labor Exhibition, however, is entirely composed of school productions, and the producers are all young students. It is truly a pure and educational exhibition. The excellence of the exhibition's achievements has been widely praised by visitors and in newspaper articles, with few criticisms. I participated in the exhibition's preparation work and visited the exhibits from various provinces and cities four or five times. Now, I will briefly present my personal observations and future hopes for consideration by experts.

Jiangsu Provincial No. 1 Middle School product (self-made exercise book)

(1) Personal Observations

A total of 29,705 exhibits were displayed in this exhibition (exhibits from the four northeastern provinces arrived after the opening, and the number was not included). Zhejiang Province had the most types of exhibits, with 37 types, followed by Shandong, with 36 types, then Jiangsu, Shanghai, and Qingdao, each with between 20 and 30 types. Ningxia, Qinghai, and Weihaiwei had the fewest, each with less than 10 types. Fujian Province had the most exhibits, with 3,213 pieces, followed by Zhejiang, with 2,694 pieces, then Shanghai and Qingdao, each with over 2,400 to over 2,600 pieces. Ningxia had the fewest, with 20 pieces. Looking at the number and types of achievements in this exhibition, one can get a glimpse of the state of labor education and vocational education development. At least, the number of types of achievements can indicate whether or not attention is being paid to labor education and vocational education, regardless of quality. In terms of quantity, there are also exceptions. For example, Guangdong Province is generally recognized as having a very developed secondary education, but only 140 items were sent to this exhibition, which is too few. Therefore, the exhibits in this exhibition do not seem to represent its overall achievements. In terms of schools participating in the exhibition, there are 266 vocational schools nationwide, and 169 participated, accounting for about 60 percent. There are 1,893 middle schools nationwide, and 337 participated, accounting for about 18 percent. There are 867 normal schools nationwide, and 139 participated, accounting for about 16 percent. There are 258,064 elementary schools nationwide, and 868 participated, accounting for about 0.3040 percent. This shows that the exhibits can only represent the overall achievements. This is probably inevitable due to practical difficulties.

In terms of schools, there are more exhibits from middle schools, normal schools, and elementary schools than from vocational schools. This is based on all exhibits. Separately, some provinces and cities have more elementary school exhibits than middle school, normal school, and vocational school exhibits, such as Shanghai and Nanjing. Some have more vocational school exhibits than primary and secondary schools, such as Hunan. Some have more middle school exhibits than vocational school and elementary school exhibits, such as Guangdong. In terms of the nature of the exhibits, industrial arts are the most common, followed by home economics, and agricultural science is the least common. China is an agricultural country, but agricultural achievements are so few, which is truly regrettable. Rice, wheat, silk, and tea are the major agricultural products of our country, but tea was not seen at all in this exhibition, which is a pity. In terms of the categories of exhibits, handicrafts are more common than mechanical industries, and decorations are more common than practical items. While it is necessary to promote and improve handicrafts today, large-scale production depends on mechanical industries. Decorations are needed in life, but they are not essential. We cannot but pay attention to this. The most praised exhibits include Hunan's embroidery, Fujian's lacquerware, Jiangxi's porcelain, Jiangsu's glass and pottery, Shandong's stone carvings, military models from Shanghai, Zhejiang, Henan, and other provinces and cities, various design models from Shanghai, Nanjing, Fujian, and other provinces and cities, teaching aids from Hebei and Fujian, machinery and woodworking products from the China Vocational School, applied chemistry and textile works from the vocational school attached to Hebei Institute of Technology and Hunan Advanced Industrial School, and spinning machines from the Ping City Han's Women's Vocational Supplementary School. Some are known for their special products, some for their creativity, some for their practicality, and some for their exquisiteness. They are truly excellent works that leave a deep impression.

The exhibits in this exhibition were dazzling and beautiful. Most of the works were newly made, except for a few old ones. This is generally recognized by visitors. Minister Wang's "Purpose of the Labor Exhibition" on the overview of the National Vocational School and Primary and Secondary School Labor Education Achievement Exhibition stated that the first condition for the exhibits was that they "can represent the usual general achievements, and not be specially made for the occasion." However, in our opinion, there are many that meet this condition, but it is difficult to guarantee that there are no items made specially for the occasion. What is meant by representing the usual general achievements refers to the labor achievements of students during normal teaching. If the purpose is only for the exhibition and the work is rushed and specially made, it loses the meaning of education and the original intention of labor.

This Labor Exhibition shows the achievements of the exhibits, not the achievements of the entire labor education. It can be said to be an exhibition of labor works, but not an exhibition of the entire labor education achievements. This is because not all labor education achievements can be shown by exhibits. For example, the classroom cleaning, arrangement, management, and decoration of school affairs work in the elementary school curriculum standards, the division of labor, management, design, decoration, and repair of school buildings, school grounds, and teaching aids, the investigation of objects in home affairs work, the investigation of the lives of farmers in agricultural work, and the investigation of the lives of workers in handicraft work can only be shown in words or reports, and there are no concrete works like woodworking and bamboo work. Also, such as the sowing, transplanting, cultivation, weeding, fertilization, pest control, and harvesting of agriculture in the middle school curriculum standards, and the home care and child rearing in home affairs, there are no concrete objects to show their achievements, and they cannot all be sent to the venue. Therefore, this exhibition is an exhibition of labor works, not an exhibition of the entire labor education achievements. After visiting, we can only say how the labor works of a certain school are, or how the labor works of a certain province are. It is not reasonable to use this to precisely evaluate the entire labor education achievements.

The schools participating in this exhibition are vocational schools, middle schools, normal schools, and elementary schools, which are all within the scope of general education and do not involve higher education. In my personal opinion, vocational education and labor education are not limited to one stage of general education. The entire school system should be labor-oriented and production-oriented. The labor education theorist Blonsky said, "Industrial education is the highest labor education." We can see from his words that vocational education is not limited to vocational schools, and labor education is not limited to primary and secondary schools. Agricultural and industrial sciences in colleges and universities can also be included in the scope of vocational education and labor education. In recent years, the central government has restricted liberal arts and promoted practical sciences, with the aim of creating practical talents to meet the needs of the country and society. The so-called practical science education is advanced vocational education and advanced labor education. If the practical science products of colleges and universities are displayed together, so that visitors can have a comprehensive concept and comparison of the production operations of schools at all levels, it would be more meaningful and valuable than this exhibition.

(2) Future Hopes

The lack of machine products and agricultural products in this Labor Exhibition has been briefly described above. Local traditional handicrafts must be improved, and machine production is even more urgent today. Handicraft industries require large costs and slow production, while machine production is the opposite. At a time when foreign goods are pouring in and increasing, large-scale machine production is needed to save the situation. Agricultural production is related to the foundation of the country. In recent years, governments at all levels have spared no effort in promoting it, and social figures have also regarded it as the key to rural revitalization. However, the agricultural products displayed in this Labor Exhibition were very few. Even in these few exhibits, there was no special progress. In the future, industrial vocational schools should move from handicrafts to focus on machine industries, especially improving local specialties with machine production. Agricultural vocational schools should pay attention to the improvement of agricultural technology and products, especially using scientific methods to improve local native products, as the basis for rural revitalization.

In the past, vocational schools mostly relied on book lectures, or lacked sufficient equipment due to economic reasons. Those who set up industrial arts lacked complete factories, and those who set up agricultural sciences lacked large farms, so that students only had brain training and lacked hand training. Even with considerable equipment, the actual operation was done by workers, which had the same drawbacks as the lack of practice venues. In the future, vocational schools must strive to enrich equipment, so that students' hand training is more than brain training, or at least the time for hand and brain training should be equal. The practice method must be like workers in factories and farmers in farms. All hard work must be done by themselves and not by others. In this way, the knowledge and experience gained by students will not be empty.

Labor education is a new product, and its meaning is broader than the handicrafts and crafts of the past. The handicrafts and crafts of the past cannot embrace today's labor education, but today's labor education can include the handicrafts or crafts of the past. The scope of labor education is broader, so its implementation method is also more difficult. The goal of labor education should be to cultivate children's creative abilities first and foremost, and to express their free will in labor operations. Schools should have sufficient labor equipment, such as factories, farms, and home economics practice venues, so that children can choose their own work, plan themselves, and create themselves, without being restricted by a fixed method. All labor operations in the school life environment can be used to implement labor education. If we only rely on a few hours of labor teaching, I am afraid that the goals stipulated in the curriculum standards cannot be fully achieved. Therefore, labor teaching should be linked to various subjects, so as to cultivate children's labor skills through the practice of various production labor, and establish the true meaning of labor education.

Anhui Education Department's Major Movement to Rescue Local Education Funds

▲ Contacting Nine Provinces Including Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, and Shandong to Strive for Central Support

The Anhui Education Department believes that the central government's order to abolish exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous fees has reduced nearly half of Anhui Province's 2.4 million yuan in local education funds, and the number of out-of-school children will increase by 90,000. It has submitted a request to the provincial government to forward it to the Executive Yuan for relief. The Executive Yuan has not yet approved it. The Education Department believes that this situation is not limited to Anhui Province, and has sent letters to the education departments of nine provinces, including Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Shandong, Fujian, Hunan, Hebei, Hubei, and Henan, requesting that they unite and strive for central support. There are three items for rescue: 1. The Ministry of Finance should promptly allocate funds to compensate for the reduced local education funds in various provinces, counties, and cities due to the abolition of exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous fees. 2. The abolition of exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous fees related to education funds that are limited in time should be postponed until a compensation method is found. In the future, a certain amount of compensation must be made before a certain amount of exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous fees can be reduced. 3. The central government should issue an order to various provinces to levy income tax, inheritance tax, luxury donation, and superstition donation, and designate these four taxes as special funds for local education fees in cities and counties. Nine provinces, including Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Jiangxi, have successively replied in agreement. The Anhui Education Department is now drafting a document to be sent to various provinces for review. Once they receive a reply, it will be sent to the ministry.

Free Talk

Thoughts in Literature

— Shen Du

Among the elements of literature, thought is one of them.

[Without thought content, artistic works cannot exist. Even works where the writer only respects form and does not care about content ultimately express some kind of definite thought.]

This sentence means that without thought, a work of art cannot become a work of art. Because thought is the author's view of life. Whether the view of life is explicit or implicit, it will inevitably be reflected in his work. This is because the view of life is none other than the author's personality or individuality. The author's social status will inevitably reflect his thoughts in his works, intentionally or unintentionally. Someone warns: [You cannot create in order to embody a certain kindness or to promote a certain thought, or to appreciate current works based on a certain thought!] The meaning of this warning is good, but in practice it has little meaning, because even if you want to avoid creating for some thought, your society will teach you to reflect it without resistance, and your thought has already been determined by the existence of your society. We should understand: [Poets, like ordinary people, even their thoughts and feelings are products of society.] Naturally, a literary artist is the same. The most important thing is not that creating to embody a certain thought or to promote a certain thought will lose its artistic value, but in the degree of authenticity expressed in the work. The closer it is to objective reality, the higher the artistic evaluation. So in this sense, although Balzac intentionally was an ardent supporter of the propertied society, he is still a great artist, precisely because his creation fully expressed the objective reality of the time. Similarly, we do not criticize Tolstoy. Although he was a writer of Christian thought, he is worthy of respect for expressing the reality of society.

However, [When the author describes thoughts, he must melt the thoughts into the crucible of emotion to describe them.] This is indeed a golden saying, because artists express their thoughts through images. If the author does not write through images but through theoretical proof, it will not become a work of art.

Mother and Daughter (Part 1)

— Li Huiying

The sky is her house, the earth is her bed, and the world is her home.

Her daughter is only four years old, but in her mother's arms, she has traveled to many places, tasted a lot of hardship, and come to know this turbid world.

The mother and daughter are a pair of wanderers, drifting from east to west, from north to south.

It's getting late. Perhaps the sun has not yet set on the western horizon, but the towering buildings of the city do obscure its light. At the same time, the bright electric lights on both sides of the street are flickering their eyes.

In short, another day has passed. Wanderers do not need to spend their energy calculating the days. They live one day at a time, and when twelve months pass, they add a year to their age. Wanderers' energy is only used on how not to go hungry, or how to make the hunger last a little longer.

However, as it got late, her stomach was indeed rumbling. At first, she could barely support herself and resist the emptiness in her stomach, but after a while, she couldn't do it at all. She just felt very weak, her hands had no strength, and as for her legs, moving them felt like they weighed at least a thousand pounds.

This was still bearable. She was an adult, and she knew that she was poor, that she was something worse than even a stray dog. But the child's appetite, once it surged up, had to be dealt with somehow.

In fact, the child had been calling her for quite a while, still mumbling:

[Mom, I want to eat. I, I'm hungry, my tummy's hot.]

What could she do about hunger? Her mother wasn't a rich person.

Holding the child, she sat down in a quiet place next to the mouth of the alley.

This big bed was cold. The wandering woman couldn't help but think that autumn had arrived. In the summer, the ground was as hot as fire.

She just wanted to sit down, stop the churning of her stomach, and also try to divert the child's demands with this action. What a stupid move! The child's hunger could not be masked with a single action. The child mumbled again:

[Mom, I want to eat. I, I'm hungry, my tummy's hot.]

This time, it seemed impossible not to answer. She repeated her usual words:

[Xiaochun, my good child, we'll go beg in a little while. Can you rest for a moment?]

Her tone was calm, and then, according to the old habit, she kissed the child's dirty little face hard a few times.

But, thinking about it, this child itself was such an inauspicious being. In between these ardent kisses, when she saw the child's eyes, which resembled her father's, she thought of her father.

The child's father was a good father, but he didn't have the destiny to be extravagant. It was really a coincidence that when the child was born into the world, it was the moment he left the world. So we should say that he didn't have the destiny to be a father, or rather, that the child was unlucky.

Therefore, she immediately felt a little disgust for the child in front of her.

This father's death was truly strange. He was fishing in the river, and on a clear day, suddenly wind and clouds rose up. When the raindrops fell, his fishing boat capsized into the water. Debts that he could never repay in his lifetime, those debts were like the net he used to fish, the net threads stubbornly dragging him into the river.

But even in his death, he had not finished paying off his debts. All the rotten things in the house went to the creditors, and she followed closely behind, leaving that desolate house. Thus, the mother and daughter became wanderers, becoming people with the four seas as their home.

An old woman selling sesame cakes and fried dough sticks, carrying a basket, walked slowly from afar, her selling voice unusually short. In fact, it could be said that she didn't want to open her throat, just like a comfortable and well-fed old woman didn't want to move her legs.

[Mom, the sesame cake and fried dough stick seller is here.]

The child shouted spontaneously, waving her hand, her eyes almost flying into the sky. The mother's heart was seized with anxiety. How could she now cover up the fact that she was deceiving the child? A hungry child absolutely would not easily give up the food in front of her eyes. As she was thinking, the child shouted again urgently:

[Mom, the sesame cake and fried dough stick seller is here.]

[Mom knows.]

Smiling, she reached into the pocket of her torn clothes, feeling clearly that there were still six copper coins. Six copper coins were more precious than six dollars to others. How many good words had she said, how many times had she called out to 'Sir', how many times had she knocked her head on the cement ground? Six copper coins that she had only earned today were not copper coins, they were simply gold, not sweat and blood! Was she really going to spend these six copper coins? No, spending them wouldn't fill her stomach. How could a fly swallowed into a tiger's stomach save it from hunger!

The old woman had already heard the child's second shout to her mother, so she walked forward. She didn't shy away from the mother and daughter's status, because in fact, most of her customers were people with tattered clothes, and at most, they were people who couldn't afford transactions of more than ten copper coins.

The electric lights seemed even brighter, which meant that it was getting darker everywhere. Now, it was dark.

Not a Fierce Dog

— TK

For Three Years

— Wei Zhongtian

For three years, I have been pacing on this endless wandering line, pacing, pacing across the green-edged sea, across the hungry-woven countryside, across the dark hell. A full three years of precious days have been wasted in wandering! Now I always sigh faintly! Life can age a young person, and so can wandering. For three years, I don't know how much turbulence and struggle I have gone through: the pain of hunger, the pain of loneliness, the pain of illness, the pain of love, the pain of insomnia... I have experienced them all. I don't know about people's memories. My own memories are more painful than joyful. People say I'm old, yes, I feel that way too.

I say, this is a year of wandering, and also a year of hunger. How many people flowed out from the hungry countryside, and how many people flowed out from the unevenly fat and thin big cities, but flowing in and out still empty stomachs, carrying disappointment and resentment. Like me, I have flowed for three full years, and am I not carrying this disappointed heart? Sometimes it feels very difficult to get through a day, but these three long years seem to have slipped away in an instant.

Thinking back on the changes in my life during these three years, sometimes I can't even believe it myself. I once lived in a world without sun for several months, eating cold rice, sleeping on the floor, listening to the moans of the sick, and watching the hideous smiles of the jailers. At night, everyone was telling their sad fate. I also wore a slanted leather belt in the gray crowd, fought battles, and saw countless dead people, corpses, and purple blood. A iron bird dropped a pile of shit and destroyed the lives of dozens of people. I have also seen it. I am not a hard-hearted person, but at that time seeing one or several dead people felt like seeing a few frogs dying on the edge of the field. Later, I hid under the wings of a peach-colored loving goddess for a while, but soon I was determined to jump out. I felt that it was not bad for young people to have this kind of life, but it was impossible to hide for a long time, so I estranged her again and embarked on the journey again. I have deeply experienced the taste of other painful things such as illness, hunger, loneliness, and insomnia, but these situations cannot be described in detail in this short article.

X X X

Until recently, my wandering life seems to have come to a small end, and by chance I came to another country to study. A person's life is really unpredictable. Sometimes it feels a bit like a dream, even I can't predict it. This time, my coming east is like this. Is it lucky? No, it cannot be said that way. Maybe there are more tragic situations waiting for me in the future. Who knows what will happen in the future? But at the moment, thinking of the bloodstains of struggling over the past few years, and now having the opportunity to relive this student life, when I walk through that narrow path full of red leaves to school every day with my schoolbag, I always feel infinitely happy!

Tokyo, December 1934

From Hekou to Lao Cai

— Li Qiao

Stepping off the train with luggage in hand, weary from a sleepless night, we tentatively set foot on the soil of Hekou, feeling somewhat lost!

Is Hekou really like this? Such a dilapidated and somewhat decadent small town, with a sparse population, only one relatively bustling street. Alongside the street stood a few huge, lush green trees. Walking on this street under the scorching sun felt strangely cool; however, a foul, miasmic odor constantly assaulted our senses, seeming like the fragrance of the trees' flowers, yet also like the stench of feces from a toilet. This smell truly made us feel somewhat afraid upon inhaling it!

Following the clerk from the shop, we arrived at the Hekou Superintendent's Inspection Office. First, we had our exit passports inspected. The inspector, like a teacher in school quizzing students, asked us about our hometowns and what we were doing in the provinces. Then, with an arrogant tone, he said:

"Alright, since that's the case, we won't make things difficult for you. Otherwise, all travelers to Hekou would have to be detained in Hekou for a day, waiting for a slow inspection before being allowed to go to Lao Cai the next day! You're getting special treatment."

As he spoke, he looked at us with cunning eyes, as if expecting some reward from us. However, we only offered a grateful smile, collected our belongings, and hurried away.

The weather in Hekou was unexpectedly so hot; after walking around the street, we were drenched in sweat, our sweat-soaked shirts sticking uncomfortably to our backs. That foul, miasmic odor kept assailing us, making us reluctant to linger any longer. With a mix of apprehension and excitement, we stepped onto the iron bridge, more than forty feet long, leading to a foreign land, without any reluctance to leave Yunnan, and headed towards Lao Cai, which radiated the majesty of imperialism.

Lao Cai, this town squatting beside the Red River, watching Hekou with a predator's gaze, doesn't seem to have a larger population than Hekou. The street is just as singular. Here, besides the shops mostly run by our countrymen from Guangdong, there are also many gambling stalls.

There are more than a dozen gambling dens, with dark crowds surrounding them, gambling on the streets day and night. Because of the hot weather, a grass mat was hung over the gambling area as a substitute for an electric fan, with someone specifically pulling it to generate refreshing breezes.

Next to the gambling dens were opera performances that could be watched without charge. The actors were all dressed strangely, performing what seemed to be Vietnamese plays. Their acting was so humorous that it was truly laughable!

This entertainment was entirely set up for the gamblers. Those who gambled spent their days with their heads down, immersed in the act, without any inclination to look up and watch. Therefore, the performances were treated like children playing around, with the players haphazardly going through the motions.

As soon as we set foot on this foreign land, a burly Vietnamese soldier stood at the end of the bridge, casting a foreign gaze at us, which made us feel somewhat fearful. We knew that inspections here were very strict. It was said that not only those carrying opium would be arrested and thrown into a water prison, but even those carrying matches would be severely punished. These rumors had made us somewhat afraid in the past, and now, stepping onto this foreign soil, our hearts couldn't help but beat faster.

Not far from the bridge, directly across the street, was a small Western-style house. Inside sat a Frenchman, resembling a judge, whose demeanor was so dignified that people dared not look him directly in the eye. The clerk guided us here, where we underwent a rigorous inspection (fortunately, we weren't carrying anything prohibited, thank God!). After our passports were checked, we were finally able to return to the shop in peace.

The weather was truly hot, and even drinking water constantly didn't quench our thirst. In the evening, when the weather cooled down a bit, three young men, draped in clothes, ran to the iron bridge shrouded in the night, bathed in the cool river breeze, listening to the sound of the Red River roaring, as if crying out for the injustices suffered by the Vietnamese people. At that moment, we felt a sense of sorrow for this foreign land.

Tomorrow (10)(4)

— (Josephcornad) Translated by Wu Xiangyu

"Hey, Dad, let me in. It's Harry, it's really me! I've only come home for a [very short time]."

One of the windows upstairs was opened.

"It's a prank, you messenger," Old Haggett's voice said from the darkness above. "You have nothing to do with him. This will ruin everything."

She heard Harry Haggett say, "Hello, Dad," followed by a "clang." The window slammed shut, and he stood before her again.

"Dad is still the same. He used to forbid me from running away, almost whipping me to death. Now that I'm back, he's trying to throw a shovel at my head to stop me from entering. The shovel grazed my shoulder blade."

She shuddered.

"I don't care," you began to say, "but I spent the last of my money on the train ticket, the last two pence on grooming! Out of respect for the old man."

"Are you really Harry Haggett?" she asked quickly. "Can you prove it?"

"Can I prove it? Who else could prove it?" he said cheerfully.

"Prove it with what? Why should I need to prove it? Except for England, perhaps nowhere else in the world could you find a man, or especially a woman, who remembers that I'm Harry Haggett. I might resemble Harry Haggett more than anyone alive; I can prove everything in a minute if you let me into your house."

"Come in," she said.

He then walked into the front garden of Garvell's house. His tall shadow strode forward, and she waited with her back to the window, watching the figure. In that figure, only the sound of approaching footsteps seemed the most real. Light shone on the wide-brimmed hat; a strong shoulder appeared, seeming to cut through the darkness; a foot stepped forward. He turned around and stood still, facing the window of the parlor, which reflected light behind her, turning his head left and right, smiling softly to himself.

Renewed Buying Spree for U.S. Dollar Silver Stocks

Yesterday (the 10th), New Far East Trading Co. reported that the New York stock market saw a mixed, slight increase led by silver stocks. News from the steel industry was unusually favorable, and according to various sources, silver advocates in the next Congress will propose a bill to mint hard currency. This led to renewed buying in gold and silver stocks. It is also rumored that investment trusts are now investing in gold mining stocks to hedge against future inflation. The bond market experienced turbulence, with foreign public bonds being particularly weak. This was attributed to Mussolini's order last Saturday, which was widely seen as an effort to prevent Italian gold from flowing out of the country. The small exchange market was stable, with a total of 850,000 shares traded throughout the day. The Dow Jones New York Index is listed below:

Yarn and Cotton

[PCurrent Sales Are Brisk, but the Yarn Market's Atmosphere Fails to Be Stimulated

The yarn market is weakening, with the situation slightly soft. However, current yarn sales are still brisk. Henan province in particular has a strong appetite for 17-count yarn, with purchases totaling 2,300 to 2,400 bales. However, market sentiment has failed to be stimulated, as some are waiting to sell when prices rise. This has resulted in a loosening of the surface, and the market has turned downward.

The Golden Rooster Falls Slightly by More Than Half a Yuan

The open of the morning yarn auction was influenced by a slight five-pound increase in US cotton and the favorable closing trend of the previous day. However, new buyers in the market were not strong, with prices for each month rising slightly by two to three jiao. As the auction reached the second and third sessions, it became increasingly soft, as some were selling when prices rose, resulting in ample supply in the market. Consequently, prices for each month fell again by three, four, five, or six jiao. The market situation remained flat at the afternoon opening. However, current yarn sales still exceeded 3,000 bales. Nevertheless, market sentiment failed to be stimulated, and prices for each month fell again by one, two, or four jiao. Sold were: Jifeng 550 bales, Dafeng 900 bales, Jinchang 400 bales, Minghua 650 bales, Gengfeng 1,650 bales, Changfeng 1,700 bales, Renfeng 650 bales, and Tonghe 650 bales. Cotton Prices Decline Along with Gold Prices

The cotton market is weakening further. Although US cotton prices rose by five basis points, the decline in gold prices and the strengthening of the US dollar exchange rate are softening sentiment. According to news from a cotton industry organization, the inventory of cotton in the Northwest is ample, and most of it has not yet been shipped out. There is hope for a continued influx in the future. However, the Tongcheng Company and the Tongzhou Syndicate are absorbing quantities of cotton and are not releasing it.

Zheng Biao Cotton Falls Back by Four to Five Jiao

The morning cotton auction opened with the US cotton market remaining calm. However, one Hankou syndicate, facing financial difficulties, has gone bankrupt. They have fully offset and settled their short position of 30,000 dan of cotton. The market atmosphere was still good in the first two sessions, but it suddenly turned downwards in the third session. This was due to the gold price breaking the 70 yuan mark and the strengthening of the exchange rate, which led to more aggressive selling. Prices for all months fell by two to three jiao. In the afternoon, news emerged of a cotton merchant selling off, further weakening the market. The price for the current month fell by 0.35 yuan, and prices for distant months fell by 0.1-0.2 yuan. Sold were: Tongji 1,300 dan, Dafu 12,400 dan, Dafeng 1,000 dan, Gengfeng 6,100 dan, Runkang 1,900 dan, Yifeng 2,700 dan, Yikang 2,800 dan, Changhe 2,900 dan, Tongfeng 3,000 dan, Renfeng 1,000 dan, Tongxing 1,900 dan, Changfeng 1,500 dan. The World Cotton Market Sees Little Glory or Disgrace

Yesterday, when the US cotton market opened, prices rose by one to four basis points due to brokerage firms and fellow traders selling short, and good weekend business news. Except for sales to the government, the amount of selling was limited. Subsequently, due to a lack of trading, the market situation was mixed and slightly soft. Fellow traders are waiting for developments. The closing was still tight and stable, with spot prices up by five basis points, and futures prices up by one to five basis points. British cotton spot prices were unchanged, and futures prices rose or fell by one point. Indian cotton was weak initially due to short selling, but rebounded due to purchases by European exporters and brokerage firms. Profits from Grain are Mostly Given Back, Flour and Wheat Prices Soften

After the flour market opened in the morning, the prices for each month showed a pattern of large increases followed by small declines. The price of foreign wheat in Chicago fell slightly by 0.25 to 1.5 cents, while Canadian wheat fell by 1-2 cents. When prices opened, the market weakened as factories slightly lowered prices and some profits were given back step by step. As for the factories, they remained wary of selling due to the uncertainty of the tax rate, so the trend remained sluggish and the decline was limited. When the market opened in the afternoon, it was initially stable due to the active current sales of the northern syndicate. Although the market looked slightly better, it was later reported that the factories had continued to order a shipment of foreign wheat at a price of 4.80 yuan, which caused prices to fall again. Given the dwindling inventory of domestic wheat, the future looks bleak without the supply of foreign wheat. As a result, the price for the current month fell slightly by 0.01 yuan, December and January fell by 0.0125 yuan, and March and May fell by 0.125 yuan.

After the wheat market opened in the morning, the prices for each month generally showed a flat and weak trend. The price of foreign wheat in Chicago fell slightly by 0.25 to 1.5 cents, while Canadian wheat fell by 1-2 cents. When prices opened, trading for each month was still active, but prices fell back as profits were given back, with near and distant months falling by 3-4 cents from the previous day. When the market opened in the afternoon, the price for the current month rose by 2-3 cents due to tighter spot prices, and sentiment gradually stabilized. The prices for distant months were initially good, but the market weakened slightly due to news that the factories had continued to order a shipment of foreign wheat and profits were being given back. As a result, the price for the current month rose by 0.02 yuan, January fell by 0.02 yuan, and February and March fell by 0.01 yuan. In the current market, the demand from factories is good and inventories are low. The price of special-grade wheat has risen by 3-4 cents. For example, high-quality Guide wheat is priced at 4.09 yuan, Xuzhou wheat is priced at 4.07 yuan, Bengbu wheat is priced at 4.05 yuan, Shuixikou wheat is priced at 4.06 yuan, Yangzhou wheat is priced at 3.95 yuan, Suzhou wheat is priced at 4.05 yuan, and Hankou wheat is priced at 3.85 yuan, with a secondary grade priced at 3.82 yuan. Fuxin purchased 5,000 bags, Fufeng purchased 2,000 bags, Shenda purchased 1,000 bags, and Xinda purchased 2,000 bags.

Chicago wheat was initially weak due to a lack of outside speculation, but prices turned flat due to a noticeable reduction in the available supply.

Rice from He Xia Continues to Arrive in a Rush, Prices Continue to Fall

(Shanghai South) Yesterday, the source of supply for various syndicates increased, with nearly 50 arrivals, mostly late rice. Therefore, the late rice market continued to show a downward trend. However, the sales market still seemed to react as it did before, losing momentum once prices fell. Customer syndicate demand was more active today, and Qingdao, Jinan, Tianjin, and other syndicates successively made purchases, with a total of more than 2,000 bags entering the market, which made the situation seem lively. However, prices had already fallen by 0.1-0.15 yuan and did not rebound. Arrivals and sales of thick japonica rice were balanced, and the market color turned stable. There was no glory or disgrace for various varieties such as Du Yang Jian and Yin Yuan, as supply and demand were similar.

(Shanghai North) Yesterday, more than 20 ships arrived from He Xia. Sales of goods in the market were sluggish in the morning for white japonica early rice but improved in the afternoon. Early thin rice and various Jian, Yin, and Yuan varieties had normal sales. Prices in the white japonica market fell slightly in the early market, but tightened in the afternoon. The price of early thin rice fell slightly. The situation for other goods was similar.

30,000 Bags of New Siamese Rice Arrive

▲ Rough Ke Xian Retreats Slightly by Nearly 0.1 Yuan

Yesterday, the demand for foreign rice remained strong, and there was an upward trend in the market. However, two ships of 4-grade rice are scheduled to arrive in Shanghai soon, and a ship of Siamese rice arrived yesterday, carrying 30,000 bags of various machine-processed broken and whole rice. Therefore, the market stabilized. Domestic demand for machine-processed rice was strong, but foreign merchants continued to sell off, and囤户 were not strongly holding on. Yesterday, 1,800 tons of new trade were sold, and 300 tons were recovered. Another small transaction of 1,000 tons was made in the evening. Both inflows and outflows were active, and the market was settled. With a continuous stream of Ke Xian rice arriving in recent days, the prices of rough and machine-processed rice had risen sharply in recent days. However, with 7,000-8,000 bags arriving yesterday, demand from buyers weakened, and the market fell slightly by nearly 0.1 yuan. The machine-processed Xian rice market was stable, with sales mainly in the Shanghai streets and inland areas. Yesterday, Tianjin purchased 500 bags of machine-processed Jiang rice and 400 bags of machine-processed Yuan rice.

Bran Inventory is Not Thick

▲ However, Yesterday's Price Fell Slightly by Two to Three Cents

The bran market has been slightly weak recently, as the inland sales channels are not active and Dongzhuang has also temporarily stopped. Compared to the previous week, prices have fallen slightly by two to three cents. Miscellaneous brands are priced at 2.72-2.73 yuan, while Hua Feng and Fu Xin bran are priced at around 2.80 yuan. However, the inventories of various factories are thin, so the future is not expected to be very low. However, the current market price is too high, and domestic consumption may be hesitant to proceed.

Soybeans Continue to Rise, Sesame Sales are Brisk

| Rumors of a 40% Reduction in Oil Tax |

Yesterday, the soybean market remained strong. Supplies were limited and inflows were not abundant. In addition to continuous demand from Zhejiang Shaoxing and Shanghai, demand from Wenzhou and Taizhou increased. Yesterday, Hankou soybeans rose by 0.13-0.14 yuan, with over 4,000 bags traded at prices ranging from 3.52 to 3.53 yuan. Over 1,500 bags of medium and high-quality Hankou soybeans were traded at prices ranging from 3.52 to 3.58 yuan, with prices rising by 0.04-0.05 yuan. 400 bags of Haocheng soybeans were traded at prices ranging from 3.68 to 3.62 yuan, with prices rising by 0.06-0.07 yuan. Over 400 bags of Xin'anzhen soybeans were offered at prices ranging from 3.64 to 3.62 yuan, also rising by 0.06-0.07 yuan. The quality of Guide soybeans was lower, and the market also rose by 0.02-0.03 yuan, with 700 bags traded. The sales channels included inland factories in Shanghai, Wenzhou, and Taizhou. In the afternoon, rumors circulated that the import tax on oil, calculated as 15% of the value after adding tariffs, might be reduced by 40%. This caused the standard oil price to fall. The Ewo Foreign Firm sold 800 tons of sesame seeds the day before yesterday at a price of 9.50 yuan. Yesterday, due to the decline in the gold price and exchange rate fluctuations, the telegram quoting 9.50 yuan had not been confirmed at the closing of the market and no transaction was made. A total of 650 bags of Jiujiang sesame seeds, 700 bags of Bengbu sesame seeds, 1,600 bags of Taizhou sesame seeds, 1,000 bags of Suzhou sesame seeds, 50 bags of Dede sesame seeds, 300 bags of Liuhe sesame seeds, and 460 bags of Yingzhou sesame seeds, and 40 bags of Bengbu yellow sesame seeds were offered (see market price column). The sales channels included traders purchasing to make 洋莊 goods, as well as cart workshops in Zhejiang and Shaoxing.

Wax Industry Sets List Prices

Yesterday, the local wax industry association continuously received news from Hankou, saying that old oil in the production area had already diminished. Although new goods have been introduced, the source of supply has been limited. In addition, the demand from various syndicates is strong, and buyers are holding back in anticipation of higher prices. Therefore, Jingshan hemp oil has been following the price increases, and the association has set list prices to notify all members to comply. The discussion is as follows: Heavy Jing without wood is priced at 19 yuan per 石, famous Jing is priced at 18.8 yuan per 石, ordinary Jing is priced at 18 yuan per 石, Macheng (market jin per dan) is priced at 17 yuan, and Sichuan (market jin) is priced at 104 yuan.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Small Talk

Matters of Human Nature and the World

— Whistle

What is meant by "matters of human nature and the world"? "Matters of human nature and the world" are originally a type of "art of living." But if we wish to study the "art of living," we must first meticulously study "matters of human nature and the world." What is meant by "human nature?" It refers to the common dispositions and temperaments of humankind. What is meant by "worldly wisdom?" It refers to the constantly evolving and bizarre states that society presents.

Human nature is about "seeking good fortune and avoiding misfortune." Towards auspicious matters, we should flock like ducks, and towards inauspicious matters, we should take flight far away, thus "turning misfortune into good fortune." Human nature is about "fearing the strong and bullying the weak." We must not provoke strong friends, lest we "pat flies on a tiger's head." It's permissible to manipulate weaker friends, as they are powerless to resist, which is called "smart people don't suffer immediate losses." Human nature is about "shying away from difficulty and enjoying ease." Therefore, everyone strives to do easy things, while difficult things are met with folded arms and indifference, allowing us to avoid "bumping our heads."

There are many such examples of human nature. Here, I have only briefly cited a few as rules. After understanding "human nature," we then play it out in society scene by scene, which is called "worldly wisdom." Therefore, if one deeply understands the changes in "matters of human nature and the world," then "the way to conduct oneself is half-considered." But simply knowing is not enough; one must also "practice it with the principle of forgiveness." Suppose I believe something is ominous, difficult, or hard to do. Not only will I not do it myself, but I will also advise others not to do it. Suppose I believe something is auspicious, soft, and easy to do. I will do it first and invite everyone to join me.

Therefore, to study the "art of living," one must first be familiar with "matters of human nature and the world." Because by being familiar with "matters of human nature and the world," one knows the methods of "seeking" and "avoiding," and the ways of "welcoming" and "rejecting." But if one is too familiar with human nature and the world, one will inevitably "anticipate others' wishes" everywhere, and "live under the thumb of others" in everything, completely losing the ability to act autonomously. There will only be objective opinions, with no subjective existence, and life will be entirely mechanical. If one is not familiar with "matters of human nature and the world," one will often encounter obstacles in speaking and acting, which is what is called "young and inexperienced," "not knowing how to read the room," or "not being able to see which way the wind blows." Not only will things not be accomplished, but one will also be ridiculed and harshly criticized. Such people are called "blockheads."

Does this mean that being familiar with "matters of human nature and the world" is bad, and not being familiar with them is also bad? How are we supposed to conduct ourselves? The ancients had a good analogy for "the way to conduct oneself," saying that it is like a copper coin. The so-called copper coin refers to the old-style cash, not the current copper plate. Because the old-style cash had a round outer shape and a square hole, conducting oneself is like cash, requiring one to be "outwardly flexible and inwardly principled." Therefore, it occurs to me that conducting oneself in the past was like cash, while conducting oneself now is like copper plates, because they are only round and have no squareness. Is there a satirical meaning in abolishing cash and using copper plates? Some people also say that conducting oneself is like "gambling." Conducting oneself in the past was like playing "Sixty-Four," which was fixed and unchangeable. Conducting oneself now is like playing "poker," which is all about "taking advantage of opportunities." Victory goes to those who can seize opportunities, and failure goes to those who cannot. This analogy is quite reasonable. Although these two matters are small, they can also greatly reflect the current "matters of human nature and the world."

But, in the end, one cannot rely entirely on "seizing opportunities," nor can one be completely "smooth." Conducting oneself should be equipped with three essential conditions: first, to clearly distinguish right from wrong; second, to recognize the truth; and third, to understand the trends of the times. If one can understand these three conditions, it is fine whether one knows "matters of human nature and the world" or not. Because the degradation of Chinese character and the decline of ambition are mostly due to being too familiar with "matters of human nature and the world."

Between Husband and Wife

— Qichang

This was an early winter night, the wind howling. He had been running around all day, hitting several snags, and had not found any money. He also failed to rent a house. He knew that if he went back like this, his wife would definitely start a quarrel, but because he was hungry, and also because he didn't want his wife to wait too long, he had no choice but to drag his heavy feet from North Sichuan Road back to their apartment in the French Concession.

The apartment was quiet. Under the dim light, only a dozing tea boy was squatting in the corner, waiting for the guests' calls. Everything was deathly silent. With a heart full of shame, he blankly walked into the dilapidated apartment, stepping into the room that was half the size of an attic. His wife was already lying in bed asleep. Although she knew he had come in, she silently rolled her eyes and pretended to be asleep. Was she really angry? He wondered, but he couldn't help but speak:

"Lan! Are you not feeling well? Have you eaten?"

Getting no response, he put on a smiling face, sat on the edge of the bed, and continued to ask, stroking her hair:

"Lan! Are you not feeling well? Have you eaten?"

"What is feeling well or not feeling well? Since I married you, have I had a single day of feeling well? This time we came back to Shanghai, I thought I could have some comfortable days, but who knew we wouldn't even have a home, living in such a dirty apartment and suffering like this!" As she spoke, her stern tone gradually softened, and she finally cried.

"Lan! Don't be sad anymore. What does such a small setback matter? We can settle down in the next day or two and get our lives in order. Believe me, we have a solution for everything!"

"What solution? I've suffered enough this year! But haven't you been saying everything has a solution? To be honest, I'm not a child anymore. These words are only good for fooling yourself!"

"When have I ever intended to deceive you? You have to understand that in this kind of society, finding a job is not easy! But everything will be resolved in a couple of days. Don't worry. Lan! Don't be so childish. Let's discuss and plan everything slowly! ... Have you eaten?"

"Who even wants to eat? What time is it? It's fine if you don't mention it, but as soon as you do, I wish I could kill you! I can tolerate the physical suffering because you're unemployed and we have financial difficulties. But I can't stand the mental anguish. Think about it: like today, from morning until now, being trapped alone in this dilapidated little room, alas! It's so hard to bear! I used to hear people say that the worst thing is being in prison, but today I want to say that the most painful thing in life is being me today..." She sobbed as if she had suffered some great injustice.

He had been running around outside all day, hitting several snags, and had been holding back a bellyful of frustration, looking for a place to vent it. But when he saw his wife's sadness, and thought about their happiness and future, he had to suppress his anger. He had always been a very easygoing person when it came to life. So, since losing his job last year, he had suffered mostly disasters this year, making him feel that the only person in this world who could sympathize with him and share his hardships was his wife. Therefore, he deeply sympathized with his wife's pain and anger. He tried hard to forget the pain of reality and pursue the happiness of the future. This future happiness was like the electric rabbit in a dog race, tempting him ahead. Therefore, even when he was exhausted, he still tightly chased after it, rushing towards the light of the future. This gave him some comfort. He thought, he forgave his wife's quarrel and patiently comforted her:

"Stop quarreling, Lan! Tomorrow we'll settle down, and everything will be fine. Get up and eat quickly, it's getting late."

He had to put on a happy face in front of his wife and ordered two meals to eat with her.

Having a Car but No Title

The Art of Getting Along in the World

— Yafei

In this day and age, everything is difficult, especially getting along in the world. The first problem in getting along in the world is eating. Originally, in these times when there is a panic about eating everywhere, eating is really not an easy thing. So, if you don't eat, how can you get along in the world? This really makes people sigh, "It's easy to be a person, but difficult to get along in the world!"

If eating is difficult, then getting along in the world is naturally even more difficult. If you act too fiercely, you will suffer at the hands of others. If you act too kindly, you won't be able to grab a job. If you are neither kind nor fierce, then perhaps people will say you are a half-wit. So I say: It is extremely difficult to get along in the world now. Being tough doesn't work, and being soft doesn't work either. Brute force and barbarism are ineffective, and yielding and giving in are even worse. Alas! How difficult it is to be a person today!

In the past, heroes created the times, but now the times create heroes. Because it is not easy to get along in the world, it has enabled experts who understand the art of getting along in the world and are good at using the methods of ascending to success to be the first to arrive, strutting around as if they were great men of the times. Those who are not familiar with the threshold of this path can only "watch others soar through the clouds."

In fact, getting along in the world is not such a difficult thing. It's just that we dullards were born with an unlucky life, so it is like this. Otherwise, since our parents gave birth to us, and our innate five senses and four limbs are all complete, we already look like a human being. Since we have the conditions for getting along in the world, why worry about not succeeding? This is certainly due to a lack of research on the cultivation of "getting along." Therefore, although we have the form of getting along, we have not yet acquired the substance of getting along. Like a "monkey wearing a hat," we look at ourselves and think we are very important, happily believing that we have indeed become a person. But in the eyes of others, we are still just a hairy-faced, sharp-mouthed monster.

Of course, I understand that to get along in the world, you must understand the art of getting along. But even if you understand it like a blind person listening to a lecture, and you don't know how to use it, or you don't use it properly, isn't it still a waste of effort? Although everyone knows that currying favor with the powerful and flattering smiles are the best ways to get ahead, I have also put in a lot of effort into this. At the time, I really wanted to "study hard for ten years without anyone asking, and become famous overnight." But the reality was the opposite of my ideal. Not only does this method not work now, but also poor kids run into walls everywhere, getting a nose full of ash.

Because I wanted to become a perfect modern man, I have been diligently studying the art of getting along in the world for the past three years, sparing no effort. Although I have not succeeded myself, I want to create a group of smart readers. Those who are interested may as well try to apply the methods. They are tested and proven a hundred times over. Anyway, I have a fearless spirit of sacrifice, but there are only notes, and no lectures. The courses are listed below:

The art of flattery, the method of bragging, the cultivation of a thick skin, the practice of scheming, the pluralistic theory of personality, the training of patience, and the secrets of prying open back doors. If you can fully learn this supreme art, I believe that not only will you be able to get along in the world with satisfaction and be welcomed and supported everywhere, but you will also have no worries about food and clothing for the rest of your life. You may even be promoted and get rich. You can get whatever you want easily. If you want to "make a living with a skill," this is the only way.

For those who are interested, we will give away a "mask" and a "General Introduction to the Art of Getting Along in the World," which are priceless. The supply is limited, so hurry, hurry.

Mary

— Ying Jiang

Isn't it strange? Because I played a "street person" for a day, everyone calls me "Mary." Not only do the people in the drama club call me that, but even those unfamiliar college students do. Sometimes they even follow behind me and ask, "Where did your John go?" to tease me, which is really embarrassing! But, after a long time, it feels very natural, and the name "Mary" naturally replaced my real name. Okay, now "Mary" is my name, but I can't bear a tragedy like the one in "Street People." I always think this way.

I remember one day, because I was bored at home, I braved the heavy snow and ran to the drama club to play. As soon as I stepped into the door, a surge of warmth rushed to my heart, because the room was full of vibrant energy. A group of young drama enthusiasts – the mustachioed director, the effeminate makeup artist, the silly old general affairs officer, the backstage boss who played the mother, and my handsome John – were sitting around the stove, talking loudly. Seeing me come in, John shouted out without hesitation: "Ah! Mary, it's so cold outside! Why did you run out?" I took off my coat, sat down next to the stove, and answered him with the lines from "Street People": "Yes, it's really cold outside. But what can I do? You know, I rushed out when the theater closed. I ran all the way to the entrance of the Paris Theater, braving the snow, begging the gentlemen, ladies, and madams who came out of the theater to give me a franc or two to support my Mary. But I begged and pleaded, running after their cars, letting the mud splash on my clothes. In the end, the answer they gave me was not the francs I was hoping for, but a rude scolding! Damn it! One day..." I had just recited to this point when the effeminate makeup artist cut in with a strange accent: "One day, one day what do you plan to do?" The shameless John snatched to answer: "One day, Mary and I will have a little baby!" This made everyone laugh, but it made me so angry that I wanted to die. I said, "John! If you are so immoral, I will never pay attention to you again!" John was busy apologizing to me, saying nice things. This kid is really annoying, always making people's hearts itch... In fact, this little John is strangely interesting and lovable! I thought this way, and my cheeks began to burn red. But, when I turned my face and saw the square-faced silly general affairs officer, my heart turned cold, and the shyness I felt just now was replaced with a sense of disgust. He always stared at me with his eyes, like a hungry wolf. Especially when I thought of his past ugly behavior of pursuing me, it was really disgusting. The backstage boss mother asked this and that like a mother asking about family matters, planning the work of the drama club. The mustachioed director was always teaching me earnestly like a teacher. To be honest, my success on the stage was also because of him. So, I respected and feared him, and sometimes I even called him "Dad." The makeup artist, although he was an effeminate person, was a pervert, like a clown. In the end, John was still a little bit lovable. But, I don't want to be Mary in "Street People." I always think this way.

The Male Heart

— Song Yuan

I no longer wish to associate with you.

You gave me a kind of temptation that will gradually cause me to lose my male self-esteem and surrender. I will not do this.

Since last summer, after I became friends with you in that small house on XX Road, I have already learned through observation and investigation that you are a woman with a decadent consciousness, a poor environment, lonely and helpless, and putting on the airs of a young lady. I also know that you have already reached the brink of financial collapse, but you lied to me about having a certain amount of savings and wanting to do something in society. This kind of fallen social butterfly's trick gave me an impression that was both laughable and pathetic. Moreover, you have already become disillusioned and depressed, to the point where you are about to fall into the vortex of ordinary women's pleasures. However, you are pretending to be a woman with a future in front of me, with amazing thoughts, which made me despise you even more in my heart. At that time, since I understood everything about you, I naturally did not succumb to your sweet words and physical temptations.

But at the same time, I really pitied you and was willing to help you do some work in social affairs. Therefore, I persuaded you to embark on the path of literature, revised your articles for you, taught you to study books, and also spent a lot of effort, hoping that you would achieve something. My view is that a woman who has worked hard in the revolutionary cause has been trained in her thinking and ideas. She can always wake up and turn back from the brink of the abyss of decline. Moreover, she is also a woman who loves literature and art, so she can always wholeheartedly dedicate herself to the literary and artistic movement, stabilize her wild and unrestrained mind, excite her feelings of moving forward and upward, and become a literary and artistic apprentice who is hardworking, able to endure hardship, and diligent in learning, in order to achieve success in literature and art.

But you have disappointed me!

You have no confidence in literature. You do not study and learn attentively. The articles you write are so hasty and careless. You do not carefully revise them to achieve true goodness and beauty. You just write a bit when you are happy, and that is it. You do not even revise them a second time. It is completely a game of pen and ink for idle people, not the serious attitude of a literary apprentice in learning to write literary works. Although you have published a few works in newspapers and magazines, they are not the kind of things you want, but you think you are satisfied and do not want to work hard to create successful works. Moreover, recently you have not even been working hard at writing. The success of a writer is not so easy, but you take the fame of a writer too lightly and do not consider the efforts of others to be such a big deal. Although the current Chinese literary world is full of smog and the Shanghai School writers are emerging one after another, exhibiting ugliness everywhere, there are still writers who can be respected and writers who are striving upwards. You cannot despise the entire Chinese literary world because of the contemptible Shanghai School writers. In particular, you cannot despise the creation of literary works because the Shanghai School writers become famous quickly.

However, you despise the entire literary world, and therefore you despise the creation of literary works even more. You have disappointed me.

If I were a female worshiper, naturally, you would have captured my heart long ago. But you have not tried to understand me and think that I am just like ordinary men. You are also going to be disappointed in me.

The male heart is more rational and self-respecting than your female heart. If he feels that he can use reason to fight against emotions, and that he has already conquered emotions, then he will embark on the path of reason and not look back.

You must know that the male heart is: career is more important than love.

Goodbye, friend! When you discover that the person you are pursuing has disappeared, you should use your smart brain to study the reasons for your failure, which will be beneficial to you. Otherwise, you will fall into an unrecoverable state.

I will tell you one last sentence: the tricks you use on men are actually not very clever. They are so hypocritical and so foolish!

Yu Xiaoxia, Yu Xiaoyun, Jade Dragonfly

New Sound (1380) 6:00 PM to 7:00 PM

Opening [Shuangwen Worships the Moon]

Waiting for the Moon in the West Chamber, the moon gradually rises, Hongniang follows the young lady. The young lady is Wang Zan, head adorned with flawless jade. Two golden hairpins divide the cloud-like temples. Double pearl earrings sway. White silk shirt emits a unique fragrance. Wang wears a pair of gold bracelets on her arm. Her chest is adorned with dazzling clothing beads. A silk handkerchief is held in her slender hands. Pink trousers bind her slender waist. Cleansing knees, with silk ribbon. Red floral shoes, spotless. Walking to the pavilion, she stops. Nine lotus lanterns hang high in front of the pavilion. Green moss sleeps with white rabbits. Wind blows butterflies dreaming in the shade of flowers. Red pear trees are full of red pear blossoms. Special red flowers wither, the peony pavilion. Locked cloud terrace, lazy to play the piano. Banana leaf fan chases fireflies. I am ten thousand miles away to meet Zhang Junsan. Zhang Sheng meets a kindred spirit in the Buddhist hall. Retiring the rebel soldiers, his merits are displayed in the Kirin Pavilion. He is like Kong Ming in the Romance of the Three Kingdoms. Tonight, the bright moon shines in the Weak Green Garden. Kneeling on a brocade cushion, secretly confessing sincerity. Wishing to pluck laurel branches in the moon palace, climb the gold list. A skillful marriage, flower candles tied together. Forever united, a century-long marriage.

National Studies

Miss Wang Bingmei's Tang Poetry

Huaxing (1260) 9:00 AM to 10:00 AM

Sent to Li Danyuanyuan Xi Wei Yingwu

Last year, I met you among the flowers, Today, the flowers bloom again after a year.

The world is vast and difficult to predict, Spring sadness is bleak, and I am the only one who is blind.

My body is full of diseases, and I think of the fields and villages, I am ashamed to receive my salary while wandering.

I heard that you want to come and ask, How many times will the moon be round in the West Building?

Same Title, Immortal Tour View Han Yi

The fairy platform first saw the Five Cities Tower, The scenery is bleak, and the rain has just stopped.

The mountain colors are connected remotely, the trees are late, The sound of the hammer is close, reporting the autumn of the Han Palace.

Sparse pine shadows fall on the empty altar, quiet, Fine grass and spring fragrance, a secluded small cave.

Why bother to look for a place outside the world, There is also a Danqiu in the human world.

Spring Thoughts Huangfu Ran

Orioles sing and swallows speak, reporting the New Year, Horses are far away, the Dragon Mound road is thousands of miles.

Living in the city near the Han Garden, My heart follows the bright moon to the land of the Hu.

The brocade letters in the loom discuss endless hate, The flowers on the building laugh at my lonely eyes.

May I ask Yuan Rong's precious chariot, When will you return to Yan Ran?
